( 2006a ) but [38;5;14muses[0m [38;5;7ma[0m more realistic [38;5;10matmospheric[0m [38;5;11mstate[0m [38;5;14mto[0m constrain the retrieval . [38;5;7mA[0m [38;5;9mdescription[0m of the [38;5;13mmethodology[0m and an [38;5;9merror[0m [38;5;11manalysis[0m are [38;5;10mpresented[0m . Single [38;5;10mdaily[0m [38;5;13mprofile[0m [38;5;9mprecision[0m [38;5;10muncertainty[0m , when taking the ascending-descending ( day-night ) [38;5;11mdifference[0m , was found [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mbe[0m [38;5;13mup[0m [38;5;14mto[0m 40 [38;5;13mpptv[0m while systematic [38;5;9merror[0m [38;5;9mbiases[0m were [38;5;13mestimated[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mbe[0m [38;5;14mless[0m [38;5;14mthan[0m about 3 [38;5;13mpptv[0m . [38;5;10mMonthly[0m [38;5;9mmean[0m comparisons show [38;5;10mbroad[0m agreement with other [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;13mwell[0m [38;5;8mas[0m with state-of-the-art numerical [38;5;13mmodels[0m . We infer [38;5;7ma[0m 2005 [38;5;10myearly[0m [38;5;10mtotal[0m [38;5;8minorganic[0m Bryusing the [38;5;13mmeasured[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;1mBrO[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mbe[0m 20.3 & amp ; plusmn ; 4.5 [38;5;13mpptv[0m , which implies [38;5;7ma[0m contribution [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;10mvery[0m [38;5;10mshort[0m [38;5;10mlived[0m [38;5;8msubstances[0m [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;8mbromine[0m [38;5;9mbudget[0m of 5 & amp ; plusmn ; 4.5 pptv. < /p >

[38;5;10mDiurnal[0m [38;5;6mvariation[0m of [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m and [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;8mHOCl[0m , [38;5;1mClO[0m and [38;5;1mHO2[0m at the [38;5;13mequator[0m : comparison of 1-D [38;5;13mmodel[0m calculations with [38;5;14mmeasurements[0m [38;5;14mby[0m [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;8minstruments[0m . Abstract . The [38;5;10mdiurnal[0m [38;5;6mvariation[0m of [38;5;8mHOCl[0m and the [38;5;14mrelated[0m [38;5;8mspecies[0m [38;5;1mClO[0m , [38;5;1mHO2[0m and [38;5;1mHCl[0m [38;5;14mmeasured[0m [38;5;14mby[0m [38;5;7msatellites[0m has been compared with the [38;5;11mresults[0m of [38;5;7ma[0m one-dimensional photochemical [38;5;13mmodel[0m . The study compares the [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m various limb-viewing [38;5;8minstruments[0m with [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;13msimulations[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;10mmiddle[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m . [38;5;13mData[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m three sub-millimetre [38;5;8minstruments[0m and two [38;5;10minfrared[0m spectrometers are [38;5;14mused[0m , [38;5;9mnamely[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the Sub-Millimetre Radiometer ( [38;5;2mSMR[0m ) on board Odin , the [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) on board [38;5;4mAura[0m , the Superconducting Submillimeter-wave Limb-Emission Sounder ( SMILES ) on the [38;5;4mInternational[0m [38;5;4mSpace[0m [38;5;4mStation[0m , the [38;5;2mMichelson[0m [38;5;2mInterferometer[0m [38;5;2mfor[0m [38;5;2mPassive[0m [38;5;2mAtmospheric[0m [38;5;1mSounding[0m ( [38;5;2mMIPAS[0m ) on board [38;5;4mENVISAT[0m , and the [38;5;2mAtmospheric[0m [38;5;2mChemistry[0m [38;5;2mExperiment[0m [38;5;2mFourier[0m [38;5;2mTransform[0m [38;5;2mSpectrometer[0m ( [38;5;2mACE-FTS[0m ) on board SCISAT . Inter-comparison of the [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;8minstruments[0m on sun-synchronous [38;5;7msatellites[0m ( [38;5;2mSMR[0m , [38;5;2mMLS[0m , [38;5;2mMIPAS[0m ) and [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m solar occultation [38;5;8minstruments[0m ( [38;5;2mACE-FTS[0m ) is challenging since the [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m correspond [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;11mdifferent[0m solar [38;5;9mzenith[0m [38;5;9mangles[0m ( or [38;5;13mlocal[0m [38;5;13mtimes[0m ) . However , [38;5;14musing[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m which [38;5;7mcovers[0m all solar [38;5;9mzenith[0m [38;5;9mangles[0m and [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the SMILES [38;5;8minstrument[0m which [38;5;13mmeasured[0m at all [38;5;13mlocal[0m [38;5;13mtimes[0m over [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mperiod[0m of [38;5;10mseveral[0m [38;5;10mmonths[0m [38;5;10mprovides[0m the possibility [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;13mverify[0m the [38;5;13mmodel[0m and [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;13mindirectly[0m compare the [38;5;10mdiurnally[0m [38;5;6mvariable[0m [38;5;8mspecies[0m . The [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m were [38;5;9maveraged[0m for [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m of 20° [38;5;8mS[0m [38;5;14mto[0m 20° [38;5;8mN[0m for the SMILES [38;5;11mobservation[0m [38;5;10mperiod[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m November 2009 [38;5;14mto[0m April 2010 and were compared at three [38;5;9maltitudes[0m : 35 , 45 and 55 km . Besides [38;5;10mpresenting[0m the SMILES [38;5;13mdata[0m , the study also shows [38;5;7ma[0m first comparison of the latest [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m ( [38;5;13mversion[0m 3.3 ) of [38;5;8mHOCl[0m , [38;5;1mClO[0m , and [38;5;1mHO2[0m with other [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m , [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;13mwell[0m [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;7ma[0m first [38;5;11mevaluation[0m of [38;5;1mHO2[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m made by Odin/SMR . The MISU-1D [38;5;13mmodel[0m has been carefully initialised and run for [38;5;9mconditions[0m and [38;5;9mlocations[0m of the [38;5;11mobservations[0m . The [38;5;6mdiurnal[0m [38;5;6mcycle[0m features for the [38;5;8mspecies[0m [38;5;11minvestigated[0m here are [38;5;13mgenerally[0m [38;5;13mwell[0m reproduced by the [38;5;13mmodel[0m . The [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m and the [38;5;13mmodel[0m agree [38;5;13mwell[0m in terms of absolute [38;5;9mmixing[0m [38;5;9mratios[0m . The [38;5;11mdifferences[0m between the [38;5;13mday[0m and night [38;5;13mvalues[0m of the [38;5;13mmodel[0m are in good agreement with the [38;5;11mobservations[0m although the [38;5;9mamplitude[0m of the [38;5;1mHO2[0m [38;5;10mdiurnal[0m [38;5;6mvariation[0m is 10–20 % [38;5;10mlower[0m in the [38;5;13mmodel[0m than in the [38;5;11mobservations[0m . In particular , the [38;5;13mdata[0m offered the opportunity [38;5;14mto[0m study the [38;5;12mreaction[0m ClO+HO2 → HOCl+O2 in the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m at 55 km . At this [38;5;9maltitude[0m the [38;5;8mHOCl[0m night-time [38;5;6mvariation[0m [38;5;10mdepends[0m only on this [38;5;12mreaction[0m . The [38;5;11mresult[0m of this [38;5;11manalysis[0m [38;5;13mpoints[0m towards [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;13mvalue[0m of the [38;5;9mrate[0m [38;5;13mconstant[0m within the [38;5;14mrange[0m [38;5;14mof[0m the JPL 2006 recommendation and the [38;5;10mupper[0m [38;5;10muncertainty[0m limit of the JPL 2011 recommendation at 55 km .

For [38;5;8mH2O[0m , upper-stratospheric and [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;6mtrends[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m GOZCARDS 1992–2010 [38;5;13mdata[0m are [38;5;10mnear[0m zero ( within ∼0.2 % yr−1 ) and [38;5;10msignificantly[0m smaller than [38;5;6mtrends[0m ( within ∼0.4–0.7 % yr−1 ) [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m for 2005–2014 or 2005–2018 . We note that the [38;5;10mvery[0m [38;5;10mshallow[0m [38;5;1msolar[0m [38;5;1mflux[0m [38;5;14mmaximum[0m [38;5;14mof[0m [38;5;6msolar[0m [38;5;6mcycle[0m 24 has contributed [38;5;14mto[0m fairly [38;5;10mlarge[0m short-term [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m and upper-stratospheric [38;5;8mH2O[0m [38;5;6mtrends[0m since 2005 . However , given [38;5;10mknown[0m [38;5;6mdrifts[0m in the [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;8mH2O[0m [38;5;13mtime[0m [38;5;13mseries[0m , [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;8mH2O[0m [38;5;6mtrend[0m [38;5;11mresults[0m , especially after 2010 , should [38;5;8mbe[0m viewed [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;10mupper[0m limits . The [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m also show [38;5;10mregions[0m and [38;5;10mperiods[0m of [38;5;10msmall[0m [38;5;1mHCl[0m [38;5;14mincreases[0m [38;5;14min[0m the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m , within the context of the longer-term [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;14mdecrease[0m [38;5;14min[0m [38;5;1mHCl[0m , [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;13mwell[0m [38;5;8mas[0m interhemispheric–latitudinal [38;5;11mdifferences[0m in short-term [38;5;1mHCl[0m [38;5;9mtendencies[0m . We [38;5;11mobserve[0m similarities in such short-term [38;5;9mtendencies[0m , and interhemispheric [38;5;10masymmetries[0m therein , for lower-stratospheric [38;5;1mHCl[0m and [38;5;1mHNO3[0m , while [38;5;1mN2O[0m [38;5;6mtrend[0m [38;5;13mprofiles[0m exhibit anti-correlated patterns.In terms of the [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;11mevaluation[0m , [38;5;6mclimatological[0m [38;5;6maverages[0m for 2005–2014 [38;5;14mfrom[0m both FR-WACCM and SD-WACCM for [38;5;1mO3[0m , [38;5;8mH2O[0m , [38;5;1mHCl[0m , [38;5;1mN2O[0m , and [38;5;1mHNO3[0m compare favorably with [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;14maverages[0m [38;5;14mover[0m this [38;5;10mperiod[0m . However , the [38;5;13mmodels[0m at mid- [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;7mhigh[0m [38;5;7mlatitudes[0m overestimate [38;5;9mmean[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m LS [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;13mvalues[0m and [38;5;10mseasonal[0m [38;5;9mamplitudes[0m by [38;5;8mas[0m much [38;5;8mas[0m 50 % –60 % ; such [38;5;11mdifferences[0m appear [38;5;14mto[0m implicate , in part , [38;5;7ma[0m transport-related [38;5;13mmodel[0m issue . At lower-stratospheric [38;5;10mhigh[0m southern [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m , [38;5;6mvariations[0m in [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;13mwinter[0m and [38;5;1mspring[0m [38;5;1mcomposition[0m [38;5;11mobserved[0m by [38;5;2mMLS[0m are [38;5;13mwell[0m matched by SD-WACCM , with the [38;5;5mmain[0m exception [38;5;8mbeing[0m for the early [38;5;13mwinter[0m [38;5;9mrate[0m of [38;5;14mdecrease[0m [38;5;14min[0m [38;5;1mHCl[0m , which is too [38;5;10mslow[0m in the [38;5;13mmodel[0m . In [38;5;13mgeneral[0m , we find that the latitude–pressure distributions of [38;5;10mannual[0m and semiannual [38;5;1moscillation[0m [38;5;9mamplitudes[0m [38;5;13mderived[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m are properly captured by the [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;9mamplitudes[0m . In terms of [38;5;10mcloseness[0m of [38;5;13mfit[0m diagnostics for model–data [38;5;10manomaly[0m series , not surprisingly , SD-WACCM ( driven by realistic [38;5;11mdynamics[0m ) [38;5;13mgenerally[0m matches the [38;5;11mobservations[0m better than FR-WACCM does . We also [38;5;14muse[0m [38;5;8mroot[0m [38;5;9mmean[0m [38;5;10msquare[0m [38;5;6mvariability[0m [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;7ma[0m more valuable [38;5;9mmetric[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;11mevaluate[0m model–data [38;5;11mdifferences[0m . We find , most notably , that FR-WACCM underestimates [38;5;11mobserved[0m interannual [38;5;6mvariability[0m for [38;5;8mH2O[0m ; this has implications for the [38;5;9mtime[0m [38;5;9mperiod[0m needed [38;5;14mto[0m detect [38;5;10msmall[0m [38;5;6mtrends[0m , [38;5;14mbased[0m [38;5;14mon[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m predictions.The WACCM [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;6mtrends[0m [38;5;13mgenerally[0m agree ( within 2σ [38;5;10muncertainties[0m ) with the [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;6mtrends[0m , although LS [38;5;6mtrends[0m are [38;5;10mtypically[0m not [38;5;13mstatistically[0m [38;5;11mdifferent[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m zero . The [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;6mtrend[0m [38;5;10mdependence[0m on [38;5;13mlatitude[0m and [38;5;10mpressure[0m is matched quite [38;5;13mwell[0m by the SD-WACCM [38;5;11mresults[0m . For [38;5;8mH2O[0m , [38;5;2mMLS[0m and SD-WACCM [38;5;9mpositive[0m [38;5;6mtrends[0m agree fairly [38;5;13mwell[0m , but FR-WACCM shows [38;5;10msignificantly[0m smaller [38;5;14mincreases[0m ; this [38;5;10mdiscrepancy[0m for FR-WACCM is [38;5;13meven[0m more pronounced for longer-term GOZCARDS [38;5;8mH2O[0m [38;5;13mrecords[0m . The larger [38;5;10mdiscrepancies[0m for FR-WACCM likely arise [38;5;14mfrom[0m its poorer [38;5;9mcorrelations[0m with [38;5;10mcold[0m [38;5;13mpoint[0m [38;5;9mtemperatures[0m and with [38;5;1mquasi-biennial[0m [38;5;1moscillation[0m ( [38;5;1mQBO[0m ) [38;5;6mvariability[0m . For [38;5;1mHCl[0m , while some [38;5;10mexpected[0m [38;5;14mdecreases[0m [38;5;14min[0m the [38;5;5mglobal[0m LS are seen in the [38;5;11mobservations[0m , there are interhemispheric [38;5;11mdifferences[0m in the [38;5;6mtrends[0m , and [38;5;14mincreasing[0m [38;5;9mtendencies[0m are suggested in [38;5;5mtropical[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m at 68 hPa , where there is only [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mslight[0m [38;5;9mpositive[0m [38;5;6mtrend[0m in SD-WACCM . Although the [38;5;13mvertical[0m [38;5;13mgradients[0m in [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;1mHCl[0m [38;5;6mtrends[0m are [38;5;13mwell[0m duplicated by SD-WACCM , the [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;6mtrends[0m are always somewhat more [38;5;10mnegative[0m ; this deserves further [38;5;11minvestigation[0m . The original [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;1mN2O[0m [38;5;9mproduct[0m [38;5;13mtime[0m [38;5;13mseries[0m [38;5;8myield[0m [38;5;10msmall[0m [38;5;9mpositive[0m LS [38;5;5mtropical[0m [38;5;6mtrends[0m ( 2005–2012 ) , [38;5;9mconsistent[0m with [38;5;13mmodels[0m and with [38;5;9mrates[0m of [38;5;14mincrease[0m [38;5;14min[0m [38;5;5mtropospheric[0m [38;5;1mN2O[0m . However , longer-term series [38;5;14mfrom[0m the more [38;5;12mcurrent[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;1mN2O[0m [38;5;11mstandard[0m [38;5;9mproduct[0m are affected by instrument-related [38;5;6mdrifts[0m that have also [38;5;14mimpacted[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;8mH2O[0m . The LS short-term [38;5;6mtrend[0m [38;5;13mprofiles[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;1mN2O[0m and [38;5;1mHNO3[0m at midlatitudes in the two [38;5;13mhemispheres[0m have [38;5;11mdifferent[0m signs ; these [38;5;6mpatterns[0m are [38;5;13mwell[0m matched by SD-WACCM [38;5;6mtrends[0m for these species.These model–data comparisons [38;5;10mprovide[0m [38;5;7ma[0m reminder that the [38;5;1mQBO[0m and other [38;5;11mdynamical[0m factors affect [38;5;10mdecadal[0m [38;5;6mvariability[0m in [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mmajor[0m way , notably in the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m , and can thus [38;5;10msignificantly[0m hinder the goals of [38;5;10mrobustly[0m [38;5;11mextracting[0m ( and explaining ) [38;5;10msmall[0m [38;5;14munderlying[0m long-term [38;5;6mtrends[0m . The [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;13msets[0m and tools discussed here for [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;11mevaluation[0m could [38;5;8mbe[0m [38;5;12mexpanded[0m [38;5;14mto[0m comparisons of [38;5;8mspecies[0m or [38;5;10mregions[0m not included here , [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;13mwell[0m [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;14mto[0m comparisons between [38;5;7ma[0m variety of chemistry–climate [38;5;13mmodels[0m .

[38;5;8mChlorine[0m partitioning [38;5;10mnear[0m the [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m [38;5;10medge[0m [38;5;11mobserved[0m with ground-based FTIR and [38;5;7msatellites[0m at Syowa [38;5;8mStation[0m , [38;5;5mAntarctica[0m , in 2007 and 2011 . Abstract . We retrieved [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;1mvertical[0m [38;5;1mprofiles[0m of [38;5;1mO3[0m , [38;5;1mHNO3[0m , and [38;5;1mHCl[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m solar spectra taken with [38;5;7ma[0m ground-based [38;5;13mFourier[0m [38;5;13mtransform[0m [38;5;10minfrared[0m spectrometer ( FTIR ) installed at Syowa [38;5;8mStation[0m , [38;5;5mAntarctica[0m ( 69.0∘ [38;5;8mS[0m , 39.6∘ [38;5;7mE[0m ) , [38;5;14mfrom[0m March [38;5;14mto[0m December 2007 and September [38;5;14mto[0m November 2011 . This was the first [38;5;13mcontinuous[0m [38;5;13mmeasurement[0m of [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;8mspecies[0m throughout the [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;6mhole[0m [38;5;10mperiod[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;7mground[0m in [38;5;5mAntarctica[0m . We [38;5;10manalyzed[0m temporal [38;5;6mvariation[0m of these [38;5;8mspecies[0m combined with [38;5;1mClO[0m , [38;5;1mHCl[0m , and [38;5;1mHNO3[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m taken with the [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m ( [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ) [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;8msensor[0m and [38;5;8mClONO2[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m taken with the Envisat [38;5;2mMIPAS[0m ( the [38;5;2mMichelson[0m [38;5;2mInterferometer[0m [38;5;2mfor[0m [38;5;2mPassive[0m [38;5;2mAtmospheric[0m [38;5;1mSounding[0m ) [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;8msensor[0m at 18 and 22 km over Syowa [38;5;8mStation[0m . An [38;5;1mHCl[0m and [38;5;8mClONO2[0m [38;5;14mdecrease[0m occurred [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;14mend[0m [38;5;14mof[0m May at both 18 and 22 km , and eventually , in early [38;5;13mwinter[0m , both [38;5;1mHCl[0m and [38;5;8mClONO2[0m were [38;5;10malmost[0m depleted . When the [38;5;6msun[0m [38;5;6mreturned[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;5mAntarctica[0m in [38;5;1mspring[0m , enhancement of [38;5;1mClO[0m and gradual [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;10mdestruction[0m were [38;5;11mobserved[0m . During the ClO-enhanced [38;5;10mperiod[0m , [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mnegative[0m [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m between [38;5;1mClO[0m and [38;5;8mClONO2[0m was [38;5;11mobserved[0m in the [38;5;13mtime[0m [38;5;13mseries[0m of the [38;5;13mdata[0m at Syowa [38;5;8mStation[0m . This [38;5;10mnegative[0m [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m was associated with the [38;5;14mrelative[0m [38;5;9mdistance[0m between Syowa [38;5;8mStation[0m and the [38;5;10medge[0m of the [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m . We [38;5;14mused[0m MIROC3.2 chemistry–climate [38;5;13mmodel[0m ( CCM ) [38;5;11mresults[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;11minvestigate[0m the [38;5;11mbehavior[0m of whole [38;5;8mchlorine[0m and [38;5;14mrelated[0m [38;5;8mspecies[0m [38;5;14minside[0m the [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m and the [38;5;10mboundary[0m [38;5;10mregion[0m in more detail . [38;5;14mFrom[0m CCM [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;11mresults[0m , the [38;5;10mrapid[0m [38;5;6mconversion[0m of [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;1mreservoir[0m [38;5;8mspecies[0m ( [38;5;1mHCl[0m and [38;5;8mClONO2[0m ) into [38;5;8mCl2[0m , gradual [38;5;6mconversion[0m of [38;5;8mCl2[0m into [38;5;8mCl2O2[0m , [38;5;14mincrease[0m [38;5;14min[0m [38;5;8mHOCl[0m in the [38;5;13mwinter[0m [38;5;10mperiod[0m , [38;5;14mincrease[0m [38;5;14min[0m [38;5;1mClO[0m when [38;5;6msunlight[0m became available , and [38;5;6mconversion[0m of [38;5;1mClO[0m into [38;5;1mHCl[0m were [38;5;6msuccessfully[0m reproduced . The [38;5;1mHCl[0m [38;5;14mdecrease[0m [38;5;14min[0m the [38;5;13mwinter[0m [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m [38;5;5mcore[0m [38;5;13mcontinued[0m [38;5;14mto[0m occur [38;5;14mdue[0m [38;5;14mto[0m both [38;5;1mtransport[0m of [38;5;8mClONO2[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the subpolar [38;5;10mregion[0m [38;5;14mto[0m higher [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m , [38;5;10mproviding[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;9mflux[0m of [38;5;8mClONO2[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m more [38;5;6msunlit[0m [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m into the [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m , and the [38;5;10mheterogeneous[0m [38;5;12mreaction[0m of [38;5;1mHCl[0m with [38;5;8mHOCl[0m . The temporal [38;5;6mvariation[0m of [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;8mspecies[0m over Syowa [38;5;8mStation[0m was affected by both [38;5;10mheterogeneous[0m [38;5;11mchemistries[0m [38;5;14mrelated[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;1mpolar[0m [38;5;1mstratospheric[0m [38;5;1mcloud[0m ( PSC ) [38;5;6moccurrence[0m [38;5;14minside[0m the [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m and [38;5;1mtransport[0m of [38;5;7ma[0m NOx-rich [38;5;6mair[0m [38;5;6mmass[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m [38;5;10mboundary[0m [38;5;10mregion[0m , which can [38;5;10mproduce[0m additional [38;5;8mClONO2[0m by [38;5;12mreaction[0m of [38;5;1mClO[0m with [38;5;1mNO2[0m . The deactivation pathways [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;6mactive[0m [38;5;8mchlorine[0m into [38;5;1mreservoir[0m [38;5;8mspecies[0m ( [38;5;1mHCl[0m and/or [38;5;8mClONO2[0m ) were confirmed [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mbe[0m [38;5;10mhighly[0m [38;5;10mdependent[0m on the availability of [38;5;13mambient[0m [38;5;1mO3[0m . At 18 km , where most [38;5;1mozone[0m was depleted , most [38;5;1mClO[0m was converted [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;1mHCl[0m . At 22 km where some [38;5;1mO3[0m was available , an additional [38;5;14mincrease[0m [38;5;14min[0m [38;5;8mClONO2[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the prewinter [38;5;13mvalue[0m occurred , similar [38;5;14mto[0m the Arctic .

EOS [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m of [38;5;10mupper[0m [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;1mBrO[0m : Implications for [38;5;10mtotal[0m [38;5;8mbromine[0m . Our ‘ best [38;5;13mestimate[0m ’ of [38;5;10mtotal[0m [38;5;10mupper[0m [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;8mbromine[0m [38;5;9mloading[0m ( [38;5;14mbased[0m [38;5;14mon[0m JPL‐2002 kinetics with the addition of [38;5;7ma[0m BrONO2 + [38;5;8mO[0m [38;5;12mreaction[0m ) is 18.6 ± 5.5 [38;5;13mpptv[0m , for the [38;5;10mperiod[0m September 2004 [38;5;14mto[0m August 2005 , [38;5;14mfrom[0m 55° [38;5;8mS[0m [38;5;14mto[0m 55° N. This implies [38;5;7ma[0m contribution of 3.0 ± 5.5 [38;5;13mpptv[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;13msources[0m other than [38;5;10mlong[0m [38;5;10mlived[0m [38;5;1mCH3Br[0m and [38;5;1mhalons[0m . The possibility of such other [38;5;13msources[0m has been [38;5;14mraised[0m by balloon , [38;5;8maircraft[0m and [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m of [38;5;1mBrO[0m in the [38;5;10mlower[0m and [38;5;10mmiddle[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m . The [38;5;9mabundance[0m of [38;5;8mbromine[0m , particularly in the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m , is [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10msignificant[0m factor in the [38;5;9mbudget[0m of [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;8mO3[0m .

Resolving the Model-Observation [38;5;10mDiscrepancy[0m in the [38;5;5mMesospheric[0m and [38;5;5mStratospheric[0m [38;5;8mHOx[0m [38;5;11mChemistry[0m : Resolving the [38;5;10mDiscrepancy[0m in [38;5;8mHOx[0m . We [38;5;10mexamine[0m the [38;5;7mmiddle[0m [38;5;7matmospheric[0m odd‐hydrogen ( [38;5;8mHOx[0m ) [38;5;11mchemistry[0m by comparing the [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) [38;5;1mOH[0m and [38;5;1mHO2[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m with [38;5;7ma[0m photochemical [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;13msimulation[0m . The [38;5;13mmodel[0m underestimates [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m and [38;5;1mHO2[0m [38;5;10mconcentrations[0m if the [38;5;11mstandard[0m [38;5;8mchemical[0m kinetic [38;5;9mrates[0m are [38;5;14mused[0m , whether the [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;8mH2O[0m and [38;5;1mO3[0m are constrained with [38;5;11mobservations[0m or not . [38;5;14mTo[0m resolve the [38;5;10mdiscrepancies[0m , we [38;5;10madjust[0m the kinetic [38;5;9mrate[0m [38;5;13mcoefficients[0m of three [38;5;10mkey[0m [38;5;12mreactions[0m ( [38;5;8mO[0m + [38;5;1mOH[0m → [38;5;8mO2[0m + [38;5;8mH[0m , [38;5;1mOH[0m + [38;5;1mHO2[0m → [38;5;8mH2O[0m + [38;5;8mO2[0m , and [38;5;8mH[0m + [38;5;8mO2[0m + M → [38;5;1mHO2[0m + M ) and the [38;5;8mO2[0m photo [38;5;1mabsorption[0m [38;5;9mcross[0m [38;5;9msection[0m at Lyman α ( 121.57 nm ) [38;5;14musing[0m the Bayesian [38;5;11moptimal[0m [38;5;13mestimation[0m . [38;5;7mA[0m much better model‐observation agreement can [38;5;8mbe[0m achieved if the kinetic [38;5;9mrate[0m [38;5;13mcoefficients[0m for [38;5;8mH[0m + [38;5;8mO2[0m + M → [38;5;1mHO2[0m + M is [38;5;14mincreased[0m by 134–310 % , and the [38;5;8mO2[0m photo [38;5;1mabsorption[0m [38;5;9mcross[0m [38;5;9msection[0m at Lyman α is [38;5;14mreduced[0m by 33–54 % , while the kinetic [38;5;9mrate[0m [38;5;13mcoefficients[0m for [38;5;8mO[0m + [38;5;1mOH[0m → [38;5;8mO2[0m + [38;5;8mH[0m and [38;5;1mOH[0m + [38;5;1mHO2[0m → [38;5;8mH2O[0m + [38;5;8mO2[0m remain [38;5;9mconsistent[0m with the [38;5;12mcurrent[0m laboratory [38;5;13mvalues[0m . The kinetic [38;5;9mrate[0m [38;5;13mcoefficient[0m for [38;5;8mH[0m + [38;5;8mO2[0m + M → [38;5;1mHO2[0m + M requires [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mvery[0m [38;5;10mlarge[0m [38;5;10madjustment[0m beyond the [38;5;10muncertainty[0m limits recommended in the NASA [38;5;13mData[0m [38;5;11mEvaluation[0m , suggesting the need for [38;5;10mfuture[0m laboratory [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m . An alternative explanation is that the [38;5;10mradiative[0m association [38;5;12mreaction[0m , [38;5;8mH[0m + [38;5;8mO2[0m → [38;5;1mHO2[0m + [38;5;8mh[0m ν , plays [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10msignificant[0m [38;5;9mrole[0m , which has never been [38;5;13mmeasured[0m . Our [38;5;11mresults[0m demonstrate that high‐quality [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m can [38;5;8mbe[0m [38;5;14mused[0m [38;5;14mto[0m constrain photochemical [38;5;13mparameters[0m and help improve our understanding of [38;5;10matmospheric[0m [38;5;11mchemistry[0m .

Technical note : [38;5;11mEvaluation[0m of the simultaneous [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m of [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m , [38;5;1mHO2[0m , and O3under [38;5;7ma[0m photochemical [38;5;10mequilibrium[0m assumption – [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;13mstatistical[0m approach . Abstract . This Technical Note [38;5;10mpresents[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;13mstatistical[0m approach [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;11mevaluating[0m simultaneous [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m of [38;5;10mseveral[0m [38;5;10matmospheric[0m [38;5;13mcomponents[0m [38;5;14munder[0m the assumption of photochemical [38;5;10mequilibrium[0m . We consider simultaneous [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m of [38;5;1mOH[0m , [38;5;1mHO2[0m , and [38;5;1mO3[0m at the [38;5;9maltitudes[0m of the [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;7ma[0m specific example and their [38;5;13mdaytime[0m photochemical [38;5;10mequilibrium[0m [38;5;8mas[0m an [38;5;11mevaluating[0m relationship . [38;5;7mA[0m simplified algebraic [38;5;13mequation[0m [38;5;14mrelating[0m [38;5;13mlocal[0m [38;5;10mconcentrations[0m of these [38;5;13mcomponents[0m in the 50–100 km [38;5;9maltitude[0m [38;5;9mrange[0m has been [38;5;13mderived[0m . The [38;5;13mparameters[0m of the [38;5;13mequation[0m are [38;5;9mtemperature[0m , [38;5;12mneutral[0m [38;5;1mdensity[0m , [38;5;13mlocal[0m [38;5;9mzenith[0m [38;5;9mangle[0m , and the [38;5;9mrates[0m of eight [38;5;12mreactions[0m . We have performed [38;5;7ma[0m one-year [38;5;13msimulation[0m of the [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m and [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mthermosphere[0m [38;5;14musing[0m [38;5;7ma[0m 3-D chemical-transport [38;5;13mmodel[0m . The [38;5;13msimulation[0m shows that the [38;5;10mdiscrepancy[0m between the calculated [38;5;6mevolution[0m of the [38;5;13mcomponents[0m and the [38;5;10mequilibrium[0m [38;5;13mvalue[0m given by the [38;5;13mequation[0m does not exceed 3–4 % in the [38;5;10mfull[0m [38;5;14mrange[0m [38;5;14mof[0m [38;5;9maltitudes[0m [38;5;10mindependent[0m of [38;5;10mseason[0m or [38;5;13mlatitude[0m . We have [38;5;11mdeveloped[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;13mstatistical[0m Bayesian [38;5;11mevaluation[0m technique for simultaneous [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m of [38;5;1mOH[0m , [38;5;1mHO2[0m , and [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;14mbased[0m [38;5;14mon[0m the [38;5;10mequilibrium[0m [38;5;13mequation[0m taking into account the [38;5;13mmeasurement[0m [38;5;9merror[0m . The first [38;5;11mresults[0m of the application of the technique [38;5;14mto[0m MLS/Aura [38;5;13mdata[0m ( [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ) are [38;5;10mpresented[0m in this Technical Note . It has been found that the [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m of the [38;5;1mHO2[0m distribution [38;5;10mregularly[0m demonstrate [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;9maltitudes[0m of this [38;5;13mcomponent[0m 's [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m maximum.This has also been confirmed by [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;1mHO2[0m distributions and comparison with offline retrieval of [38;5;1mHO2[0m fromthe [38;5;10mdaily[0m [38;5;10mzonal[0m [38;5;9mmeans[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;9mradiance[0m .

[38;5;10mUnusual[0m [38;5;8mchlorine[0m partitioning in the 2015/16 [38;5;5mArctic[0m [38;5;13mwinter[0m lowermost [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m : [38;5;11mobservations[0m and [38;5;13msimulations[0m . Abstract . The [38;5;5mArctic[0m [38;5;13mwinter[0m 2015/16 was characterized by [38;5;10mcold[0m [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;9mtemperatures[0m . Here we [38;5;10mpresent[0m [38;5;7ma[0m comprehensive view of the temporal [38;5;6mevolution[0m of [38;5;8mchlorine[0m in the lowermost [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m over the course of the studied [38;5;13mwinter[0m . We utilize two-dimensional [38;5;13mvertical[0m [38;5;9mcross[0m [38;5;9msections[0m of [38;5;1mozone[0m ( [38;5;1mO3[0m ) and [38;5;1mchlorine[0m [38;5;1mnitrate[0m ( [38;5;8mClONO2[0m ) , [38;5;14mmeasured[0m [38;5;14mby[0m the [38;5;10mairborne[0m limb [38;5;13mimager[0m [38;5;2mGLORIA[0m ( Gimballed Limb [38;5;11mObserver[0m for [38;5;1mRadiance[0m [38;5;13mImaging[0m of the [38;5;10mAtmosphere[0m ) during the POLSTRACC/GW-LCYCLE II/GWEX/SALSA [38;5;11mcampaigns[0m , [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;11minvestigate[0m the [38;5;1mtropopause[0m [38;5;10mregion[0m in detail . [38;5;11mObservations[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m three long-distance [38;5;11mflights[0m in January , February , and March 2016 are discussed . [38;5;8mClONO2[0m [38;5;9mvolume[0m [38;5;9mmixing[0m [38;5;9mratios[0m [38;5;13mup[0m [38;5;14mto[0m 1100 [38;5;13mpptv[0m were [38;5;13mmeasured[0m at 380 [38;5;8mK[0m [38;5;1mpotential[0m [38;5;1mtemperature[0m in [38;5;10mmesoscale[0m [38;5;13mstructures[0m . Similar [38;5;10mmesoscale[0m [38;5;13mstructures[0m are also [38;5;1mvisible[0m in [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m . Both [38;5;8mtrace[0m [38;5;8mgas[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m are applied [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;11mevaluate[0m [38;5;13msimulation[0m [38;5;11mresults[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;11mchemistry[0m [38;5;1mtransport[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;1mCLaMS[0m ( [38;5;8mChemical[0m [38;5;9mLagrangian[0m [38;5;13mModel[0m of the [38;5;5mStratosphere[0m ) and the chemistry–climate [38;5;13mmodel[0m EMAC ( ECHAM5/MESSy [38;5;10mAtmospheric[0m [38;5;11mChemistry[0m ) . These comparisons show agreement within the [38;5;10mexpected[0m performance of these models.Satellite [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m Aura/MLS ( [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ) and SCISAT/ACE-FTS ( [38;5;4mAtmospheric[0m [38;5;4mChemistry[0m [38;5;4mExperiment[0m – [38;5;2mFourier[0m [38;5;2mTransform[0m [38;5;2mSpectrometer[0m ) [38;5;10mprovide[0m an overview over the whole [38;5;13mwinter[0m and information about the [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m situation [38;5;14mabove[0m the [38;5;11mflight[0m [38;5;9maltitude[0m . [38;5;13mTime[0m [38;5;13mseries[0m of these [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m reveal [38;5;10munusually[0m [38;5;10mlow[0m [38;5;8mhydrochloric[0m [38;5;8macid[0m ( [38;5;1mHCl[0m ) and [38;5;8mClONO2[0m at 380 [38;5;8mK[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;14mbeginning[0m of January [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;14mend[0m [38;5;14mof[0m February 2016 , while [38;5;1mchlorine[0m [38;5;1mmonoxide[0m ( [38;5;1mClO[0m ) is [38;5;10mstrongly[0m enhanced . In March 2016 , [38;5;10munusually[0m [38;5;10mrapid[0m [38;5;8mchlorine[0m deactivation into [38;5;1mHCl[0m is [38;5;11mobserved[0m instead of deactivation into [38;5;8mClONO2[0m , the more [38;5;10mtypical[0m pathway for deactivation in the [38;5;5mArctic[0m . [38;5;8mChlorine[0m deactivation [38;5;11mobserved[0m in the [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;13mtime[0m [38;5;13mseries[0m is [38;5;13mwell[0m reproduced by [38;5;1mCLaMS[0m . [38;5;9mSensitivity[0m [38;5;13msimulations[0m with [38;5;1mCLaMS[0m demonstrate the influence of [38;5;10mlow[0m [38;5;9mabundances[0m of [38;5;1mO3[0m and [38;5;9mreactive[0m [38;5;1mnitrogen[0m ( [38;5;8mNOy[0m ) [38;5;14mdue[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;6mdepletion[0m and [38;5;1msedimentation[0m of NOy-containing [38;5;10mparticles[0m , respectively . On the basis of the [38;5;11mdifferent[0m [38;5;9maltitude[0m and [38;5;9mtime[0m [38;5;9mranges[0m of these effects , we conclude that the substantial [38;5;8mchlorine[0m deactivation into [38;5;1mHCl[0m at 380 [38;5;8mK[0m arose [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;11mresult[0m of [38;5;10mvery[0m [38;5;10mlow[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;9mabundances[0m together with [38;5;10mlow[0m [38;5;9mtemperatures[0m . Additionally , [38;5;1mCLaMS[0m [38;5;13mestimates[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;6mdepletion[0m of at least 0.4 [38;5;13mppmv[0m at 380 [38;5;8mK[0m and 1.75 [38;5;13mppmv[0m at 490 [38;5;8mK[0m , which is comparable [38;5;14mto[0m other [38;5;10mextremely[0m [38;5;10mcold[0m [38;5;5mArctic[0m [38;5;13mwinters[0m . We have [38;5;14mused[0m [38;5;1mCLaMS[0m [38;5;13mtrajectories[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;10manalyze[0m the [38;5;13mhistory[0m of enhanced [38;5;8mClONO2[0m [38;5;14mmeasured[0m [38;5;14mby[0m [38;5;2mGLORIA[0m . In February , most of the enhanced [38;5;8mClONO2[0m is [38;5;10mtraced[0m back [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mchlorine[0m deactivation that had occurred within the [38;5;10mpast[0m few [38;5;13mdays[0m [38;5;10mprior[0m [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;2mGLORIA[0m [38;5;13mmeasurement[0m . The [38;5;1mhydroxyl[0m radical [38;5;8mas[0m an [38;5;10mindicator[0m of SEP [38;5;9mfluxes[0m in the high-latitude [38;5;10mterrestrial[0m [38;5;10matmosphere[0m . The [38;5;10mlow[0m [38;5;13mbackground[0m [38;5;13mvalues[0m at [38;5;13mnighttime[0m of the [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mhydroxyl[0m ( [38;5;1mOH[0m ) radical make it easier [38;5;14mto[0m single out the [38;5;10matmospheric[0m response [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;13mexternal[0m [38;5;1msolar[0m [38;5;1mforcing[0m in [38;5;5mPolar[0m [38;5;10mRegions[0m . Because of the [38;5;10mshort[0m [38;5;10mlifetime[0m of [38;5;8mHOx[0m , it is possible [38;5;14mto[0m follow the trails of [38;5;8mSolar[0m [38;5;8mEnergetic[0m [38;5;8mParticle[0m ( SEP ) [38;5;6mevents[0m in the [38;5;10mterrestrial[0m [38;5;10matmosphere[0m , [38;5;8mas[0m shown by Storini and Damiani ( 2008 ) . The [38;5;9msensitivity[0m of this [38;5;10mindicator[0m makes discernible not only [38;5;10mextreme[0m [38;5;10mparticle[0m [38;5;6mevents[0m with [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;9mflux[0m [38;5;9mpeak[0m of [38;5;10mseveral[0m thousand pfu [ 1 pfu = 1 particle/ ( cm2 [38;5;8ms[0m sr ) ] at [38;5;9menergies[0m > 10 MeV , but also those with [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;9mflux[0m [38;5;13mup[0m [38;5;14mto[0m about 300 pfu . [38;5;14mUsing[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) on board the EOS AURA [38;5;7msatellite[0m , we [38;5;10mexamined[0m the [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m of [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;9mabundance[0m vs. solar [38;5;1mproton[0m [38;5;1mflux[0m for [38;5;10malmost[0m all the identified SEP [38;5;6mevents[0m spanning [38;5;14mfrom[0m November 2004 [38;5;14mto[0m December 2006 ( [38;5;9mlater[0m on [38;5;1mno[0m more SEP [38;5;6mevents[0m occurred during [38;5;6mSolar[0m [38;5;6mCycle[0m [38;5;1mno[0m . 23 ) . The [38;5;7mchannels[0m at [38;5;9menergies[0m [38;5;14mgreater[0m [38;5;14mthan[0m 5 MeV and 10 MeV showed the best [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m [38;5;13mvalues[0m ( [38;5;13mr[0m ∼ 0.90–0.95 ) at [38;5;9maltitudes[0m around 65–75 km whereas , [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;10mexpected[0m , the most energetic [38;5;7mchannels[0m were most [38;5;10mhighly[0m [38;5;9mcorrelated[0m at [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;9maltitudes[0m . Therefore , it is reasonably possible [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;13mestimate[0m the solar [38;5;1mproton[0m [38;5;1mflux[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;13mvalues[0m of [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m ( and viceversa ) and it could [38;5;8mbe[0m [38;5;14museful[0m in studying [38;5;10mperiods[0m with gaps in the [38;5;13mrecords[0m of solar particles.In addition , the SEP [38;5;6mevents[0m of September 2005 , characterized by an [38;5;11mevident[0m [38;5;13mhemispheric[0m [38;5;10masymmetry[0m of the SEP-induced [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;13mformation[0m , have been [38;5;10mexamined[0m [38;5;10mseparately[0m . Preliminary analyses performed with other [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m ( i.e. , [38;5;1mO3[0m , [38;5;8mH2O[0m , [38;5;1mT[0m ) suggest that [38;5;10matmospheric[0m [38;5;11min[0m [38;5;11msitu[0m [38;5;9mconditions[0m could play [38;5;7ma[0m relevant [38;5;9mrole[0m in explaining the [38;5;13mhemispheric[0m [38;5;10masymmetry[0m of [38;5;8mOH[0m .

The 27 [38;5;13mday[0m solar [38;5;10mrotational[0m effect on [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;13mnighttime[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m and O3observations [38;5;10minduced[0m by [38;5;1mgeomagnetic[0m [38;5;1mactivity[0m . [38;5;11mObservations[0m performed by the [38;5;7mEarth[0m [38;5;11mObserving[0m [38;5;6mSystem[0m [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m [38;5;8minstrument[0m on board the [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m 2004 [38;5;14mto[0m 2009 ( 2004 [38;5;14mto[0m 2014 ) were [38;5;14mused[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;11minvestigate[0m the 27 [38;5;13mday[0m solar [38;5;10mrotational[0m [38;5;9mcycle[0m in [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m ( [38;5;1mO3[0m ) and the [38;5;11mphysical[0m [38;5;9mconnection[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;1mgeomagnetic[0m [38;5;1mactivity[0m . [38;5;13mData[0m [38;5;11manalysis[0m was [38;5;9mfocused[0m on [38;5;13mnighttime[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m at [38;5;6mgeomagnetic[0m [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m [38;5;9mconnected[0m [38;5;14mto[0m the outer [38;5;7mradiation[0m [38;5;7mbelts[0m ( 55°N/S–75°N/S ) . The applied superposed [38;5;10mepoch[0m [38;5;11manalysis[0m reveals [38;5;7ma[0m distinct 27 [38;5;13mday[0m solar [38;5;10mrotational[0m [38;5;8msignal[0m in [38;5;1mOH[0m and [38;5;1mO3[0m during [38;5;13mwinter[0m in both [38;5;13mhemispheres[0m at [38;5;9maltitudes[0m > 70 km . The [38;5;1mOH[0m response is [38;5;9mpositive[0m and in‐phase with the respective [38;5;1mgeomagnetic[0m [38;5;1mactivity[0m [38;5;8msignal[0m , lasting for 1–2 [38;5;13mdays[0m . In contrast , the [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;6mfeedback[0m is [38;5;10mnegative[0m , [38;5;9mdelayed[0m by 1 [38;5;13mday[0m , and is [38;5;10mpresent[0m [38;5;13mup[0m [38;5;14mto[0m 4 [38;5;13mdays[0m afterward . Largest [38;5;1mOH[0m ( [38;5;1mO3[0m ) [38;5;9mpeaks[0m are found at ~75 km , exceeding the 95 % [38;5;10msignificance[0m [38;5;9mlevel[0m and the [38;5;13mmeasurement[0m [38;5;6mnoise[0m of < 2 % ( < 0.5 % ) , while reaching [38;5;6mvariations[0m of +14 % ( −7 % ) [38;5;14mwith[0m [38;5;14mrespect[0m [38;5;14mto[0m their corresponding [38;5;13mbackground[0m . [38;5;1mOH[0m at 75 km is [38;5;11mobserved[0m [38;5;14mto[0m respond [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;10mparticle[0m [38;5;6mprecipitation[0m only after [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mcertain[0m [38;5;9mthreshold[0m of [38;5;1mgeomagnetic[0m [38;5;1mactivity[0m is exceeded , [38;5;10mdepending[0m on the respective [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;13mbackground[0m . The [38;5;14mrelation[0m between [38;5;1mOH[0m and [38;5;1mO3[0m at 75 km in both [38;5;13mhemispheres[0m is found [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mbe[0m [38;5;13mnonlinear[0m . In particular , [38;5;1mOH[0m has [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mstrong[0m [38;5;14mimpact[0m on [38;5;1mO3[0m for [38;5;14mrelatively[0m [38;5;10mweak[0m [38;5;6mgeomagnetic[0m [38;5;6mdisturbances[0m and accompanying [38;5;10msmall[0m absolute [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;6mvariations[0m ( < 0.04 [38;5;13mppb[0m ) . In contrast , catalytic [38;5;1mO3[0m depletion is seen [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;10mslow[0m [38;5;13mdown[0m for stronger [38;5;6mgeomagnetic[0m [38;5;6mvariations[0m and [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;10manomalies[0m ( 0.04–0.13 [38;5;13mppb[0m ) , revealing [38;5;10msmall[0m [38;5;6mvariations[0m around −0.11 [38;5;13mppm[0m .

Spatial Heterodyne [38;5;13mImager[0m for [38;5;5mMesospheric[0m Radicals on STPSat-1 . The Spatial Heterodyne [38;5;13mImager[0m for [38;5;5mMesospheric[0m Radicals ( SHIMMER ) was [38;5;7ma[0m high‐resolution , [38;5;10mnear[0m [38;5;10multraviolet[0m spectrometer that [38;5;13mimaged[0m the [38;5;7mEarth[0m 's limb for 2.5 [38;5;10myears[0m between March 2007 and October 2009 . The [38;5;8minstrument[0m [38;5;14mused[0m the Spatial Heterodyne [38;5;13mSpectroscopy[0m technique for the first [38;5;14mtime[0m on [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;7msatellite[0m and [38;5;6msuccessfully[0m demonstrated its capabilities . SHIMMER [38;5;13mmeasured[0m the solar [38;5;10mresonance[0m [38;5;1mfluorescence[0m of the [38;5;1mOH[0m A2Σ+‐X2Π ( 0 , 0 ) band around 309 nm , which allows the retrieval of [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;1mdensity[0m [38;5;13mprofiles[0m . It also [38;5;13mmeasured[0m the [38;5;12mRayleigh[0m [38;5;1mscattered[0m [38;5;13mbackground[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;10mclear[0m [38;5;10matmosphere[0m and solar [38;5;1mscattering[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;1mpolar[0m [38;5;1mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mcloud[0m [38;5;10mparticles[0m . We [38;5;10mpresent[0m details on the SHIMMER mission , the payload design , and the [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;11manalysis[0m . [38;5;7mA[0m comparison between SHIMMER and concurrent [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m shows good agreement between 60 and 90 km [38;5;9maltitude[0m for [38;5;10mseveral[0m [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m and [38;5;10mseasons[0m . We also find good agreement of the SHIMMER [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;1mdensities[0m and [38;5;11mstandard[0m photochemical [38;5;13mmodel[0m calculations between 60 and 80 km . We find [38;5;1mno[0m [38;5;11mevidence[0m of [38;5;7ma[0m 25 % –35 % [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;10mdeficit[0m , previously reported [38;5;14musing[0m [38;5;7mMiddle[0m [38;5;7mAtmosphere[0m High‐Resolution Spectrograph [38;5;11mInvestigation[0m ( MAHRSI ) [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m . However , [38;5;10mindependent[0m [38;5;11manalysis[0m of [38;5;12mRayleigh[0m [38;5;1mscattered[0m [38;5;13mbackground[0m [38;5;8msignals[0m [38;5;11mobserved[0m by SHIMMER and MAHRSI [38;5;14munder[0m similar [38;5;10mlighting[0m [38;5;9mconditions[0m revealed that MAHRSI [38;5;1mradiances[0m are systematically smaller than SHIMMER [38;5;1mradiances[0m by 24 % . Although this [38;5;11mdifference[0m is [38;5;13mwell[0m [38;5;14moutside[0m of the combined [38;5;10muncertainties[0m for both [38;5;11mexperiments[0m , the agreement of SHIMMER [38;5;1mOH[0m with [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m and [38;5;11mstandard[0m [38;5;1mphotochemistry[0m [38;5;11mresults[0m , together with our [38;5;12mRayleigh[0m [38;5;1mscattering[0m comparison , suggests an unidentified MAHRSI [38;5;13mcalibration[0m problem that effectively eliminates the [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;10mdeficit[0m reported [38;5;14musing[0m MAHRSI [38;5;11mobservations[0m .

Spatial and Temporal [38;5;13mStructure[0m of the [38;5;10mTertiary[0m [38;5;1mOzone[0m [38;5;9mMaximum[0m in the [38;5;5mPolar[0m [38;5;13mWinter[0m [38;5;5mMesosphere[0m . [38;5;11mObservations[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;7msatellites[0m and [38;5;7ma[0m ground‐based [38;5;8mstation[0m are combined [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;10mconstruct[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;5mglobal[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;13mset[0m for [38;5;11minvestigating[0m the [38;5;10mtertiary[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;9mmaximum[0m in the [38;5;13mwinter[0m [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m for the [38;5;10mperiod[0m August 2004 [38;5;14mto[0m June 2017 . [38;5;13mSimulation[0m of [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;6mloss[0m in [38;5;5mArctic[0m [38;5;13mwinter[0m 2004/2005 : [38;5;1mOZONE[0m [38;5;6mLOSS[0m IN [38;5;5mARCTIC[0m [38;5;13mWINTER[0m 2004/2005 . We [38;5;10mpresent[0m [38;5;13msimulations[0m of [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;6mdepletion[0m in the [38;5;5mArctic[0m [38;5;13mwinter[0m 2004/2005 by the [38;5;8mChemical[0m [38;5;9mLagrangian[0m [38;5;13mModel[0m of the [38;5;5mStratosphere[0m ( [38;5;1mCLaMS[0m ) . [38;5;6mPrecipitating[0m [38;5;7mradiation[0m [38;5;7mbelt[0m [38;5;10melectrons[0m and enhancements of [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mhydroxyl[0m during 2004-2009 : [38;5;5mMESOSPHERIC[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m RESPONSE . [38;5;8mEnergetic[0m [38;5;8mparticle[0m [38;5;6mprecipitation[0m [38;5;1mleads[0m [38;5;14mto[0m enhancement of odd [38;5;8mhydrogen[0m ( [38;5;8mHOx[0m ) [38;5;14mbelow[0m 80 km [38;5;9maltitude[0m through [38;5;8mwater[0m [38;5;13mcluster[0m [38;5;1mion[0m [38;5;1mchemistry[0m . [38;5;14mUsing[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( MLS/Aura ) and [38;5;10mMedium[0m [38;5;9mEnergy[0m [38;5;8mProton[0m and [38;5;10mElectron[0m Detector ( MEPED/POES ) between 2004–2009 , we study [38;5;6mvariations[0m of [38;5;13mnighttime[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;14mcaused[0m [38;5;14mby[0m [38;5;7mradiation[0m [38;5;7mbelt[0m [38;5;10melectrons[0m at [38;5;6mgeomagnetic[0m [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m 55–65° . For those [38;5;10mmonths[0m with [38;5;10mdaily[0m [38;5;9mmean[0m 100–300 keV [38;5;10melectron[0m [38;5;9mcount[0m [38;5;9mrate[0m exceeding 150 counts/s in the outer [38;5;7mradiation[0m [38;5;7mbelt[0m , we find [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mstrong[0m [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m ( [38;5;13mr[0m ≥ 0.6 ) between [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;9mmixing[0m [38;5;9mratios[0m at 70–78 km ( 0.046–0.015 hPa ) and [38;5;6mprecipitating[0m [38;5;10melectrons[0m . [38;5;9mCorrelations[0m [38;5;13mr[0m ≥ 0.35 , corresponding [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;10mrandom[0m chance [38;5;9mprobability[0m [38;5;8mp[0m ≤ 5 % , are [38;5;11mobserved[0m [38;5;13mdown[0m to52 km ( 0.681 hPa ) , while [38;5;1mno[0m [38;5;10mclear[0m [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m is [38;5;11mobserved[0m at [38;5;9maltitudes[0m [38;5;14mbelow[0m . This suggests that the [38;5;9mfluxes[0m of ≥3 MeV [38;5;10melectrons[0m were not [38;5;10mhigh[0m enough [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;14mcause[0m [38;5;11mobservable[0m [38;5;6mchanges[0m in [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;9mmixing[0m [38;5;9mratios[0m . At 75 km , in about 34 % of the 65 [38;5;10mmonths[0m [38;5;10manalyzed[0m we find [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m [38;5;13mr[0m ≥ 0.35 . Although similar [38;5;11mresults[0m are obtained for both [38;5;13mhemispheres[0m in [38;5;13mgeneral[0m , in some cases the [38;5;11mdifferences[0m in [38;5;10matmospheric[0m [38;5;9mconditions[0m make the [38;5;1mOH[0m response more difficult [38;5;14mto[0m detect in the [38;5;13mSouth[0m . Considering the [38;5;13mlatitude[0m extent of [38;5;10melectron[0m [38;5;9mforcing[0m , we find [38;5;10mclear[0m effects on [38;5;1mOH[0m at [38;5;12mmagnetic[0m [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m 55–72° , while the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m are influenced much less . Because the [38;5;9mtime[0m [38;5;9mperiod[0m 2004–2009 [38;5;10manalyzed[0m here coincided with an extended [38;5;10msolar[0m [38;5;10mminimum[0m , and the [38;5;10myear[0m 2009 was [38;5;10manomalously[0m [38;5;10mquiet[0m , it is reasonable [38;5;14mto[0m assume that our [38;5;11mresults[0m [38;5;10mprovide[0m [38;5;7ma[0m lower‐limit [38;5;14mestimation[0m [38;5;14mof[0m the [38;5;10mimportance[0m of energetic [38;5;10melectron[0m [38;5;6mprecipitation[0m at the [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m considered .

First [38;5;11mresults[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the Spatial Heterodyne [38;5;13mImager[0m for [38;5;5mMesospheric[0m Radicals ( SHIMMER ) : [38;5;10mDiurnal[0m [38;5;6mvariation[0m of [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mhydroxyl[0m . We [38;5;10mpresent[0m the first SHIMMER [38;5;11mobservations[0m of the [38;5;10mdiurnal[0m [38;5;6mvariation[0m of [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mhydroxyl[0m ( [38;5;1mOH[0m ) . This [38;5;11mvalidates[0m the Spatial Heterodyne [38;5;13mSpectroscopy[0m technique for space‐borne [38;5;13moptical[0m [38;5;13mremote[0m [38;5;13msensing[0m applications . We extend our [38;5;11manalysis[0m [38;5;14mto[0m other [38;5;13mlocal[0m [38;5;13mtimes[0m , not [38;5;11mobserved[0m by [38;5;2mMLS[0m , for [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m [38;5;10mnear[0m 55°N in the [38;5;13msummer[0m of 2007 . At 74 km , we find excellent agreement with [38;5;7ma[0m photochemical [38;5;13mmodel[0m , but [38;5;14mabove[0m 76 km , [38;5;10msignificant[0m model/data [38;5;11mdifferences[0m in the [38;5;9mshape[0m of the [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;10mdiurnal[0m [38;5;6mvariation[0m are [38;5;11mobserved[0m .

First [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m of [38;5;1mClO[0m in the Venus [38;5;10matmosphere[0m – [38;5;9mAltitude[0m [38;5;10mdependence[0m and temporal [38;5;6mvariation[0m . The 352.88 GHz submm [38;5;1mabsorption[0m [38;5;13mspectrum[0m of 35ClO in the Venus [38;5;10matmosphere[0m was [38;5;11mobserved[0m on Oct 23 and Nov 11 , 2010 , [38;5;14musing[0m the James Clerk Maxwell [38;5;8mTelescope[0m ( JCMT ) on Mauna Kea , HI . This is the first detection of Venus [38;5;1mClO[0m , which is found [38;5;14mto[0m exhibit much larger [38;5;9mabundances[0m in the [38;5;10mupper[0m ( 85–100 km ) versus [38;5;10mlower[0m ( 70–85 km ) [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m , [38;5;10mbased[0m upon retrieval of the [38;5;9maltitude[0m distribution [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;9mshape[0m of the [38;5;10mpressure[0m broadened [38;5;1mabsorption[0m . The 2-day [38;5;9maverage[0m of all [38;5;6mcollected[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;10mindicates[0m 2.6 ±0.5 [38;5;13mppb[0m [38;5;14mabove[0m 85 ±2 km , and undetectable [38;5;14mbelow[0m . Temporal [38;5;6mvariation[0m is [38;5;11mevident[0m between the Oct 23 and Nov 11 [38;5;11mobservations[0m , which [38;5;10mindicate[0m [38;5;10mupper[0m [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;9mmixing[0m [38;5;9mratios[0m of 3.7 ±0.9 and 1.5 ±0.5 [38;5;13mppb[0m , respectively . At these [38;5;9mabundances[0m catalytic [38;5;10mdestruction[0m of [38;5;1mozone[0m by [38;5;10mhighly[0m [38;5;9mreactive[0m [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;8mcompounds[0m ( [38;5;8mClOx[0m ) must occur , reinforcing the ( Montmessin [38;5;7met[0m al. , 2011 ) [38;5;14mconclusion[0m that their [38;5;13mmeasured[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;13mprofiles[0m were [38;5;9mconsistent[0m with chlorine-catalyzed [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;10mdestruction[0m [38;5;14mabove[0m 90 km . Detection of [38;5;1mClO[0m in the nightside [38;5;10matmosphere[0m reveals that [38;5;8mClOx[0m [38;5;9mabundances[0m exceed those of [38;5;10mhighly[0m [38;5;9mreactive[0m [38;5;1mnitrogen[0m ( [38;5;1mNOx[0m ) . [38;5;10mRecent[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m of [38;5;1mHCl[0m in both the night- and day-side [38;5;10matmosphere[0m ( Sandor and Clancy , 2012 ; 2017 ) demonstrate that [38;5;10mupper[0m [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mHCl[0m [38;5;10mrepresents[0m [38;5;14mless[0m [38;5;14mthan[0m [38;5;13mhalf[0m the [38;5;10mtotal[0m [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;9mbudget[0m . This required [38;5;7ma[0m non-HCl [38;5;1mreservoir[0m [38;5;9mconsisting[0m of [38;5;10mhighly[0m [38;5;9mreactive[0m gas-phase [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;8mcompounds[0m ( [38;5;8mClOx[0m ) , [38;5;1mHCl[0m [38;5;8maerosol[0m [38;5;10mparticles[0m , or both . The [38;5;13mmeasured[0m 1.5–3.7 [38;5;13mppb[0m [38;5;1mClO[0m [38;5;13mdirectly[0m [38;5;10mindicates[0m hundreds of [38;5;13mppb[0m of [38;5;8mCl[0m , demonstrating that [38;5;8mClOx[0m ( rather than [38;5;8maerosol[0m ) is [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mprimary[0m [38;5;10mupper[0m [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;1mreservoir[0m . Finally , this first detection of [38;5;1mClO[0m constitutes the first empirical corroboration that the ( Yung and DeMore , 1982 ) chlorine-catalysis [38;5;11mmechanism[0m is responsible for [38;5;1mstabilizing[0m the Venus [38;5;10matmosphere[0m [38;5;8mas[0m 97 % [38;5;1mCO2[0m , 3 % [38;5;8mN2[0m ( rather than comparable ( within [38;5;7ma[0m factor of 2 ) [38;5;1mCO[0m , [38;5;8mO2[0m and [38;5;1mCO2[0m [38;5;9mabundances[0m ) .

Comparison of [38;5;1mClO[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m [38;5;14mto[0m ground-based [38;5;10mmicrowave[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m at Scott [38;5;10mBase[0m , [38;5;5mAntarctica[0m , in [38;5;1mspring[0m 2005 . We have [38;5;10mexamined[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m of [38;5;1mchlorine[0m [38;5;1mmonoxide[0m , [38;5;1mClO[0m , in the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m by the [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) on the [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;7msatellite[0m in the [38;5;7maustral[0m [38;5;1mspring[0m of 2005 . These [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m have been compared [38;5;14mto[0m those of [38;5;7ma[0m ground‐based spectrometer at Scott [38;5;10mBase[0m , [38;5;5mAntarctica[0m . The [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;11manalysis[0m is performed in both cases by [38;5;13msubtracting[0m [38;5;13mnighttime[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;13mdaytime[0m ones . The [38;5;10mtransition[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;10mfull[0m [38;5;10mdarkness[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;10mfull[0m daylight at the [38;5;7mhigh[0m [38;5;7mlatitude[0m of Scott [38;5;10mBase[0m limits the [38;5;14mtime[0m during which both [38;5;13mday[0m and night [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m are made . After further [38;5;6mselection[0m for good [38;5;11mobserving[0m [38;5;9mconditions[0m and the [38;5;9mposition[0m of the [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m , 16 [38;5;11mvalid[0m [38;5;13mprofile[0m comparisons are made . The day‐to‐day [38;5;6mvariability[0m of [38;5;1mClO[0m is [38;5;11mobserved[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mbe[0m [38;5;10mlarge[0m , ∼30 % of its [38;5;9mpeak[0m [38;5;13mvalue[0m . The [38;5;10mdaily[0m [38;5;13mcolumn[0m [38;5;1mdensities[0m of the two [38;5;8minstruments[0m are [38;5;9mcorrelated[0m with [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10msignificance[0m of 3σ with most of the [38;5;9mmean[0m [38;5;11mdifference[0m arising [38;5;14mfrom[0m 2 [38;5;13mdays[0m . The [38;5;13mstatistical[0m agreement between [38;5;2mMLS[0m and the Scott [38;5;10mBase[0m [38;5;8minstrument[0m is good . [38;5;11mAnalysis[0m of [38;5;10mDiurnal[0m and [38;5;10mSeasonal[0m [38;5;11mBehavior[0m of [38;5;13mSurface[0m [38;5;1mOzone[0m and Its Precursors ( [38;5;1mNOx[0m ) at [38;5;7ma[0m Semi-Arid Rural Site in Southern [38;5;5mIndia[0m . [38;5;13mSurface[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m of [38;5;1mO3[0m , [38;5;1mNO[0m , [38;5;1mNO2[0m and [38;5;1mNOx[0m have been made over [38;5;7ma[0m semi-arid rural site , Anantapur ( 14.62°N ; 77.65°E ; 331 m asl ) in southern [38;5;5mIndia[0m , during January-December 2010 . The highest [38;5;10mmonthly[0m [38;5;9mmean[0m [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;10mconcentration[0m was [38;5;11mobserved[0m in April ( 56.1 ± 9.9 [38;5;13mppbv[0m ) and the lowest in August ( 28.5 ± 7.4 ) , with an [38;5;10mannual[0m [38;5;9mmean[0m of 40.7 ± 8.7 [38;5;13mppbv[0m for the [38;5;11mobservation[0m [38;5;10mperiod[0m . [38;5;10mSeasonal[0m [38;5;6mvariations[0m in [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;10mconcentrations[0m were the highest during the [38;5;13msummer[0m ( 70.2 ± 6.9 [38;5;13mppbv[0m ) , and lowest during the [38;5;1mmonsoon[0m [38;5;10mseason[0m ( 20.0 ± 4.7 [38;5;13mppbv[0m ) , with an [38;5;10mannual[0m [38;5;9mmean[0m of 40.7 ± 8.7 [38;5;13mppbv[0m . In contrast , higher [38;5;1mNOx[0m [38;5;13mvalues[0m appeared in the [38;5;13mwinter[0m ( 12.8 ± 0.8 [38;5;13mppbv[0m ) followed by the [38;5;13msummer[0m [38;5;10mseason[0m ( 10.9 ± 0.7 [38;5;13mppbv[0m ) , while [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;13mvalues[0m appeared in the [38;5;1mmonsoon[0m [38;5;10mseason[0m ( 3.7 ± 0.5 [38;5;13mppbv[0m ) . The [38;5;11mresults[0m for [38;5;1mO3[0m , [38;5;1mNO[0m and [38;5;1mNO2[0m [38;5;10mindicate[0m that the [38;5;9mlevel[0m of [38;5;1moxidant[0m [38;5;10mconcentration[0m ( [ [38;5;8mOX[0m ] = [38;5;1mNO2[0m + [38;5;1mO3[0m ) at [38;5;7ma[0m given [38;5;9mlocation[0m is the [38;5;13msum[0m of NOx-independent “ [38;5;10mregional[0m contribution ” ( [38;5;13mbackground[0m [38;5;9mlevel[0m of [38;5;1mO3[0m ) and [38;5;13mlinearly[0m NOx-dependent “ [38;5;13mlocal[0m contribution ” . The [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;10mconcentration[0m shows [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10msignificant[0m [38;5;9mpositive[0m [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m with [38;5;9mtemperature[0m , and [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mnegative[0m [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m with both [38;5;1mwind[0m [38;5;1mspeed[0m and [38;5;1mrelative[0m [38;5;1mhumidity[0m . In contrast , [38;5;1mNOx[0m have [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10msignificant[0m [38;5;9mpositive[0m [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m with [38;5;1mhumidity[0m and [38;5;1mwind[0m [38;5;1mspeed[0m , and [38;5;10mnegative[0m [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m with [38;5;9mtemperature[0m . The [38;5;13mslope[0m between [ BC ] and [ [38;5;1mO3[0m ] suggests that every 1 μg/m3 [38;5;14mincrease[0m [38;5;14min[0m [38;5;8mblack[0m [38;5;1mcarbon[0m [38;5;8maerosol[0m [38;5;9mmass[0m [38;5;9mconcentration[0m [38;5;14mcauses[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;1mreduction[0m of 4.7 μg/m3 in the [38;5;13msurface[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;10mconcentration[0m . [38;5;7mA[0m comparative study [38;5;14musing[0m [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m shows that [38;5;10mannual[0m [38;5;9mmean[0m [38;5;13mvalues[0m of [38;5;1mtropospheric[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m contributes 12 % of [38;5;10mtotal[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m , while [38;5;10mnear[0m [38;5;13msurface[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m contributes 82 % of [38;5;1mtropospheric[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m . [38;5;7mA[0m nudged chemistry-climate [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;13msimulation[0m of [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;9mconstituent[0m distribution at northern high-latitude [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m [38;5;11mobserved[0m by SMILES and [38;5;2mMLS[0m during the 2009/2010 [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m sudden [38;5;10mwarming[0m : [38;5;7mA[0m NUDGED CCM [38;5;13mSIMULATION[0m OF THE 2010 SSW . [38;5;5mStratospheric[0m sudden [38;5;10mwarming[0m ( SSW ) is [38;5;7ma[0m dramatic phenomenon of the [38;5;13mwinter[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m in which the distribution of [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;9mconstituents[0m , associated [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;9mtendency[0m , and [38;5;1mtransport[0m of [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;9mconstituents[0m [38;5;11mdiffer[0m [38;5;10msignificantly[0m [38;5;14minside[0m and [38;5;14moutside[0m of the [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m . In this study , the [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;9mconstituent[0m distributions in the [38;5;10mmajor[0m SSW of 2009/2010 were [38;5;13msimulated[0m by the [38;5;13mModel[0m for Interdisciplinary [38;5;10mResearch[0m on [38;5;6mClimate[0m 3.2‐Chemistry‐Climate [38;5;13mModel[0m ( CCM ) nudged toward the European [38;5;9mCenter[0m for Medium‐Range [38;5;1mWeather[0m Forecasts‐Interim Re‐Analysis [38;5;13mdata[0m . The [38;5;11mresults[0m were compared with Superconducting Submillimeter‐Wave Limb‐Emission Sounder ( SMILES ) and [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) [38;5;11mobservations[0m . Those of [38;5;1mClO[0m are also similar , considering the [38;5;11mdifference[0m in the [38;5;13mlocal[0m [38;5;13mtime[0m for the [38;5;13mmeasurement[0m . Analyses of the nudged CCM run [38;5;10mindicate[0m that [38;5;14minside[0m the [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m at 50 hPa , the [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;10mconcentration[0m [38;5;14mincreased[0m [38;5;10mmoderately[0m owing [38;5;14mto[0m partial cancelation between the [38;5;10mlarge[0m [38;5;10mnegative[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;9mtendency[0m [38;5;14mdue[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;10mdestruction[0m and [38;5;10mlarge[0m [38;5;9mpositive[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;9mtendency[0m [38;5;14mdue[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;13mhorizontal[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m influx [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;14moutside[0m of the [38;5;6mvortex[0m [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;13mwell[0m [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;13mdownward[0m [38;5;1madvection[0m . [38;5;7mA[0m [38;5;10mminor[0m sudden [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;10mwarming[0m with [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mmajor[0m [38;5;14mimpact[0m : [38;5;1mTransport[0m and [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;11mprocessing[0m in the 2014/2015 [38;5;5mArctic[0m [38;5;13mwinter[0m . [38;5;5mStratospheric[0m [38;5;1mtransport[0m and [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;11mprocessing[0m during the 2014/2015 [38;5;5mArctic[0m [38;5;13mwinter[0m were [38;5;10mstrongly[0m influenced by [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mminor[0m sudden [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;10mwarming[0m ( SSW ) in early January . [38;5;6mDisturbances[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;9mtemperatures[0m and [38;5;1mtrace[0m [38;5;1mgases[0m in the [38;5;10mmiddle[0m and [38;5;10mupper[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m were similar in [38;5;13mcharacter[0m [38;5;14mto[0m those associated with [38;5;10mmajor[0m SSWs : The [38;5;1mstratopause[0m [38;5;14mdropped[0m , and [38;5;13mvertical[0m [38;5;1mtemperature[0m [38;5;1mgradients[0m weakened , followed by renewed [38;5;11mdescent[0m of [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;8mair[0m . The [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m was barely [38;5;6mdisrupted[0m and remained [38;5;10munusually[0m [38;5;10mstrong[0m throughout the [38;5;13mwinter[0m . The SSW did , however , [38;5;14mcause[0m [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;9mtemperatures[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;14mrise[0m [38;5;13mwell[0m [38;5;14mabove[0m [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;6mactivation[0m [38;5;9mthresholds[0m ; [38;5;8mtrace[0m [38;5;8mgas[0m [38;5;9mabundances[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) were consequently exceptional . The [38;5;13mdegree[0m of [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;6mactivation[0m in January was the smallest , and [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;13mvalues[0m in February were the highest , in the 11 [38;5;10myear[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;13mrecord[0m . The [38;5;10mmajor[0m [38;5;9mrole[0m played by [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mminor[0m SSW highlights the [38;5;5mArctic[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m 's [38;5;9msensitivity[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;13mspectrum[0m of [38;5;11mdynamical[0m [38;5;6mvariability[0m .

This paper reports on an [38;5;14mincrease[0m of [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;6mevent[0m [38;5;11mobserved[0m over Kerguelen ( 49.4° [38;5;8mS[0m , 70.3° [38;5;7mE[0m ) in relationship with large-scale [38;5;10misentropic[0m [38;5;1mtransport[0m . It is evidenced [38;5;14mfrom[0m ground-based [38;5;11mobservations[0m , together with [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;5mglobal[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m and [38;5;13massimilated[0m [38;5;13mfields[0m . The study is [38;5;14mbased[0m [38;5;14mon[0m the analyses of the first ozonesonde [38;5;11mexperiment[0m never [38;5;13mrecorded[0m at the Kerguelen site in the framework of [38;5;7ma[0m French [38;5;11mcampaign[0m called [38;5;8mROCK[0m that took place [38;5;14mfrom[0m April [38;5;14mto[0m August 2008 . Comparisons and interpretations of the [38;5;11mobserved[0m [38;5;6mevent[0m are supported by co-localised [38;5;2mSAOZ[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m , by [38;5;5mglobal[0m [38;5;13mmapping[0m of tracers ( [38;5;1mO3[0m , [38;5;1mN2O[0m and [38;5;13mcolumns[0m of [38;5;1mO3[0m ) [38;5;14mfrom[0m Aura/MLS and Aura/OMI [38;5;11mexperiments[0m , and by [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;13msimulations[0m of [38;5;9mErtel[0m [38;5;1mPotential[0m [38;5;1mVorticity[0m initialised by ECMWF ( European Centre for Medium-Range [38;5;1mWeather[0m [38;5;13mForecasts[0m ) [38;5;13mdata[0m reanalyses . [38;5;7mSatellite[0m and ground-based [38;5;11mobservational[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m revealed [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;9mconsistent[0m [38;5;14mincrease[0m of [38;5;1mozone[0m in the [38;5;13mlocal[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m by mid-April 2008 . Additionally , [38;5;1mOzone[0m ( [38;5;1mO3[0m ) and [38;5;1mnitrous[0m [38;5;1moxide[0m ( [38;5;1mN2O[0m ) [38;5;13mprofiles[0m obtained during January–May 2008 by the [38;5;10mMicrowave[0m Lamb Sounder ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) aboard the [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;7msatellite[0m are [38;5;13massimilated[0m into MOCAGE ( MOdèle de Chimie Atmosphérique à Grande Echelle ) , [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;5mglobal[0m three-dimensional [38;5;11mchemistry[0m [38;5;1mtransport[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m of Météo-France . The [38;5;13massimilated[0m [38;5;10mtotal[0m [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;13mvalues[0m are [38;5;9mconsistent[0m with [38;5;2mSAOZ[0m [38;5;7mground[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m ( within ±5 % ) , and [38;5;10misentropic[0m distributions of [38;5;1mO3[0m are matching [38;5;13mwell[0m with [38;5;13mmaps[0m of [38;5;1madvected[0m [38;5;1mpotential[0m [38;5;1mvorticity[0m ( APV ) [38;5;13mderived[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the MIMOSA [38;5;13mmodel[0m , [38;5;7ma[0m high-resolution [38;5;1madvection[0m [38;5;1mtransport[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m , and [38;5;14mfrom[0m ECMWF [38;5;13mreanalysis[0m . The studied [38;5;6mevent[0m seems [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mbe[0m [38;5;14mrelated[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;10misentropic[0m [38;5;1mtransport[0m of [38;5;6mair[0m [38;5;6mmasses[0m that took place simultaneously in the lower- and middle-stratosphere , respectively [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;10mregion[0m and [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;5mtropics[0m [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;5mmid-latitudes[0m . In fact , the studied [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;14mincrease[0m by mid April 2008 [38;5;11mresults[0m simultaneously : ( 1 ) [38;5;14mfrom[0m an equator-ward [38;5;11mdeparture[0m of [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mair[0m [38;5;6mmasses[0m characterised with [38;5;7ma[0m high-ozone [38;5;7mlayer[0m in the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m ( [38;5;10mnearby[0m the 475 [38;5;8mK[0m [38;5;10misentropic[0m [38;5;9mlevel[0m ) , and ( 2 ) [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mreverse[0m [38;5;10misentropic[0m [38;5;1mtransport[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;5mtropics[0m [38;5;14mto[0m mid- and high-latitudes in the [38;5;10mupper[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m ( [38;5;10mnearby[0m the 700 [38;5;8mK[0m [38;5;9mlevel[0m ) . The [38;5;14mincrease[0m of [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;11mobserved[0m over Kerguelen [38;5;14mfrom[0m the 16-April ozonesonde [38;5;13mprofile[0m is then [38;5;11mattributed[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;7ma[0m concomitant [38;5;10misentropic[0m [38;5;1mtransport[0m of [38;5;1mozone[0m in two [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;7mlayers[0m : the [38;5;5mtropical[0m [38;5;8mair[0m moving [38;5;13msouthward[0m and reaches over Kerguelen in the [38;5;10mupper[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m , and the [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;8mair[0m [38;5;7mpassing[0m over the same [38;5;9marea[0m but in the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;7mstratosphere[0m .

An [38;5;11massessment[0m of [38;5;2mCALIOP[0m [38;5;1mpolar[0m [38;5;1mstratospheric[0m [38;5;1mcloud[0m [38;5;1mcomposition[0m [38;5;13mclassification[0m . Abstract . This study [38;5;11massesses[0m the [38;5;10mrobustness[0m of the [38;5;2mCALIOP[0m ( [38;5;2mCloud-Aerosol[0m [38;5;2mLidar[0m [38;5;2mwith[0m [38;5;2mOrthogonal[0m [38;5;2mPolarization[0m ) [38;5;1mpolar[0m [38;5;1mstratospheric[0m [38;5;1mcloud[0m ( PSC ) [38;5;1mcomposition[0m [38;5;13mclassification[0m [38;5;13malgorithm[0m – which is [38;5;10mbased[0m solely on the [38;5;10mspaceborne[0m [38;5;8mlidar[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m – through the [38;5;14muse[0m of [38;5;10mnearly[0m coincident gas-phase [38;5;1mHNO3[0m and [38;5;8mH2O[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) on [38;5;4mAura[0m and Goddard [38;5;7mEarth[0m [38;5;11mObserving[0m [38;5;6mSystem[0m [38;5;13mModel[0m , [38;5;13mVersion[0m 5 ( [38;5;4mGEOS-5[0m ) [38;5;9mtemperature[0m analyses . Following the approach of Lambert [38;5;7met[0m [38;5;8mal[0m . ( 2012 ) , we compared the [38;5;11mobserved[0m temperature-dependent [38;5;1mHNO3[0m [38;5;6muptake[0m by PSCs in the various [38;5;2mCALIOP[0m [38;5;1mcomposition[0m classes with [38;5;13mmodeled[0m [38;5;6muptake[0m for supercooled ternary [38;5;13msolutions[0m ( [38;5;2mSTS[0m ) and [38;5;10mequilibrium[0m [38;5;1mnitric[0m [38;5;1macid[0m [38;5;8mtrihydrate[0m ( [38;5;8mNAT[0m ) . We [38;5;10mexamined[0m the [38;5;2mCALIOP[0m PSC [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;13mrecord[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m both [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;10mregions[0m over the [38;5;10mperiod[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m 2006 through 2011 and over [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;14mrange[0m [38;5;14mof[0m [38;5;1mpotential[0m [38;5;1mtemperature[0m [38;5;9mlevels[0m spanning the 15–30 km [38;5;9maltitude[0m [38;5;9mrange[0m . We found that most PSCs identified [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;2mSTS[0m exhibit [38;5;10mgas[0m phase [38;5;6muptake[0m of [38;5;1mHNO3[0m [38;5;9mconsistent[0m with [38;5;13mtheory[0m , but with [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10msmall[0m [38;5;9mtemperature[0m [38;5;9mbias[0m , similar [38;5;14mto[0m Lambert [38;5;7met[0m [38;5;8mal[0m . ( 2012 ) . [38;5;6mIce[0m PSC [38;5;13mclassification[0m is also [38;5;10mrobust[0m in the [38;5;2mCALIOP[0m [38;5;13moptical[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m , with the [38;5;9mmode[0m in the [38;5;6mice[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m occurring about 0.5 [38;5;8mK[0m [38;5;14mbelow[0m the [38;5;1mfrost[0m [38;5;13mpoint[0m . We found that [38;5;2mCALIOP[0m PSCs identified [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;8mNAT[0m [38;5;8mmixtures[0m exhibit two distinct [38;5;11mpreferred[0m [38;5;9mmodes[0m which [38;5;1mreflect[0m the fact that the [38;5;6mgrowth[0m of [38;5;8mNAT[0m [38;5;10mparticles[0m is kinetically limited . One [38;5;9mmode[0m is [38;5;10msignificantly[0m out of [38;5;10mthermodynamic[0m [38;5;10mequilibrium[0m [38;5;14mwith[0m [38;5;14mrespect[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mNAT[0m [38;5;14mdue[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;10mshort[0m [38;5;9mexposure[0m [38;5;14mtimes[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;9mtemperatures[0m [38;5;14mbelow[0m the [38;5;8mNAT[0m existence [38;5;9mtemperature[0m , TNAT , with [38;5;1mHNO3[0m [38;5;6muptake[0m [38;5;6mdominated[0m by the more numerous [38;5;10mliquid[0m [38;5;10mdroplets[0m . The other [38;5;8mNAT[0m [38;5;8mmixture[0m [38;5;9mmode[0m is much closer [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mNAT[0m [38;5;10mthermodynamic[0m [38;5;10mequilibrium[0m , [38;5;10mindicating[0m that the [38;5;10mparticles[0m have been exposed [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;9mtemperatures[0m [38;5;14mbelow[0m TNAT for extended [38;5;10mperiods[0m of [38;5;14mtime[0m . With [38;5;7ma[0m few notable exceptions , PSCs in the various [38;5;1mcomposition[0m classes conform [38;5;13mwell[0m [38;5;14mto[0m their [38;5;10mexpected[0m [38;5;9mtemperature[0m existence regimes . We have [38;5;7ma[0m good understanding of the [38;5;14mcause[0m of the [38;5;10mminor[0m misclassifications that [38;5;8mdo[0m occur and will [38;5;11minvestigate[0m [38;5;9mmeans[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;11mcorrect[0m these deficiencies in our next generation [38;5;13malgorithm[0m .

[38;5;7mA[0m [38;5;5mtropospheric[0m [38;5;11mchemistry[0m [38;5;13mreanalysis[0m for the [38;5;10myears[0m 2005–2012 [38;5;14mbased[0m [38;5;14mon[0m an [38;5;13massimilation[0m of [38;5;2mOMI[0m , [38;5;2mMLS[0m , [38;5;2mTES[0m , and [38;5;2mMOPITT[0m [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m . Abstract . We [38;5;10mpresent[0m the [38;5;11mresults[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m an 8-year [38;5;5mtropospheric[0m [38;5;11mchemistry[0m [38;5;13mreanalysis[0m for the [38;5;10mperiod[0m 2005–2012 obtained by [38;5;13massimilating[0m [38;5;13mmultiple[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;13msets[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;2mOMI[0m , [38;5;2mMLS[0m , [38;5;2mTES[0m , and [38;5;2mMOPITT[0m [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;8minstruments[0m . The [38;5;13mreanalysis[0m calculation was [38;5;1mconducted[0m [38;5;14musing[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;5mglobal[0m [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;1mtransport[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m and an [38;5;13mensemble[0m Kalman [38;5;10mfilter[0m technique that simultaneously optimises the [38;5;1mchemical[0m [38;5;1mconcentrations[0m of various [38;5;8mspecies[0m and [38;5;1memissions[0m of [38;5;10mseveral[0m precursors . The optimisation of both the [38;5;10mconcentration[0m and the [38;5;1memission[0m [38;5;13mfields[0m is an [38;5;9mefficient[0m method [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;11mcorrect[0m the entire [38;5;5mtropospheric[0m [38;5;13mprofile[0m and its year-to-year [38;5;6mvariations[0m , and [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;10madjust[0m various tracers [38;5;8mchemically[0m linked [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;8mspecies[0m [38;5;13massimilated[0m . Comparisons against [38;5;10mindependent[0m [38;5;8maircraft[0m , [38;5;7msatellite[0m , and ozonesonde [38;5;11mobservations[0m demonstrate the [38;5;9mquality[0m of the analysed [38;5;1mO3[0m , [38;5;1mNO2[0m , and [38;5;1mCO[0m [38;5;10mconcentrations[0m on [38;5;10mregional[0m and [38;5;5mglobal[0m [38;5;10mscales[0m and for both [38;5;10mseasonal[0m and year-to-year [38;5;6mvariations[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mtroposphere[0m [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m . The [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;13massimilation[0m [38;5;13mstatistics[0m imply persistent [38;5;1mreduction[0m of [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;9merror[0m and improved [38;5;14mrepresentation[0m [38;5;14mof[0m [38;5;1memission[0m [38;5;6mvariability[0m , but they also show that [38;5;13mdiscontinuities[0m in the availability of the [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m [38;5;1mlead[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;1mdegradation[0m of the [38;5;13mreanalysis[0m . The [38;5;14mdecrease[0m [38;5;14min[0m the number of [38;5;13massimilated[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m [38;5;14mincreased[0m the ozonesonde-minus-analysis [38;5;11mdifference[0m after 2010 and [38;5;14mcaused[0m [38;5;10mspurious[0m [38;5;6mvariations[0m in the [38;5;13mestimated[0m [38;5;1memissions[0m . The Northern/Southern [38;5;13mHemisphere[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;13mratio[0m was modified [38;5;10mconsiderably[0m [38;5;14mdue[0m [38;5;14mto[0m the multiple-species [38;5;13massimilation[0m and became closer [38;5;14mto[0m an [38;5;11mobservational[0m [38;5;13mestimate[0m , which played an [38;5;10mimportant[0m [38;5;9mrole[0m in [38;5;12mpropagating[0m [38;5;11mobservational[0m information among various [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;13mfields[0m and affected the [38;5;1memission[0m [38;5;13mestimates[0m . [38;5;7mA[0m Match-based approach [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;14mestimation[0m [38;5;14mof[0m [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;6mloss[0m [38;5;14musing[0m [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m . Abstract . The method was [38;5;10mpioneered[0m [38;5;14musing[0m ozonesonde [38;5;11mobservations[0m , for which hundreds of matched [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m per [38;5;13mwinter[0m are [38;5;10mtypically[0m available . The [38;5;10mdense[0m coverage of the [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m , particularly at [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m , allows matches [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mbe[0m made [38;5;14mto[0m thousands of [38;5;11mobservations[0m each [38;5;13mday[0m . Applying Match calculations [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m of [38;5;1mnitrous[0m [38;5;1moxide[0m , [38;5;7ma[0m long-lived tracer whose [38;5;10mexpected[0m [38;5;9mrate[0m of [38;5;6mchange[0m is negligible on the [38;5;10mweekly[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;10mmonthly[0m timescales considered here , enables quantification of the [38;5;14mimpact[0m of [38;5;1mtransport[0m [38;5;9merrors[0m on the Match-based [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;6mloss[0m [38;5;13mestimates[0m .
