Comparisons against the Whole [38;5;10mAtmosphere[0m [38;5;9mCommunity[0m [38;5;13mClimate[0m [38;5;13mModel[0m ( WACCM ) , the Superconducting Submillimeter-Wave Limb-Emission Sounder ( SMILES ) and the [38;5;10mFar[0m [38;5;10mInfrared[0m Spectrometer ( FIRS-2 ) [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m , [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;13mwell[0m [38;5;8mas[0m photochemical [38;5;13msimulations[0m , demonstrate the [38;5;10mrobustness[0m of the retrieval and [38;5;10mindicate[0m that the retrieval is [38;5;9msensitive[0m enough [38;5;14mto[0m detect [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mHO2[0m [38;5;7mlayers[0m during both [38;5;13mday[0m and night . This [38;5;10mnew[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;13mset[0m is the first long-term [38;5;1mHO2[0m [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m and [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;13mrecord[0m and it [38;5;10mprovides[0m needed constraints [38;5;14mto[0m help resolve the [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;10mdeficit[0m problem and the `` [38;5;8mHOx[0m dilemma '' .

[38;5;6mSignature[0m of the 27-day solar [38;5;10mrotation[0m [38;5;9mcycle[0m in [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m and [38;5;8mH2O[0m [38;5;11mobserved[0m by the [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m . Abstract . The [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mhydroxyl[0m radical ( [38;5;1mOH[0m ) is [38;5;5mmainly[0m [38;5;10mproduced[0m by the [38;5;1mwater[0m [38;5;1mvapor[0m ( [38;5;8mH2O[0m ) [38;5;12mphotolysis[0m and could [38;5;8mbe[0m considered [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mproxy[0m for the influence of the [38;5;1msolar[0m [38;5;1mirradiance[0m [38;5;6mvariability[0m on the [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m . We [38;5;10manalyze[0m the [38;5;5mtropical[0m [38;5;9mmean[0m response of the [38;5;5mmesospheric[0m [38;5;1mOH[0m and [38;5;8mH2O[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;11mobserved[0m by the [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) [38;5;14mto[0m 27-day solar [38;5;6mvariability[0m . The [38;5;11manalysis[0m is performed for two [38;5;9mtime[0m [38;5;9mperiods[0m corresponding [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;11mdifferent[0m phases of the 11-yr [38;5;9mcycle[0m : [38;5;14mfrom[0m December 2004 [38;5;14mto[0m December 2005 ( the [38;5;10mperiod[0m of `` [38;5;10mhigh[0m [38;5;6mactivity[0m '' with [38;5;7ma[0m pronounced 27-day [38;5;6msolar[0m [38;5;6mcycle[0m ) and [38;5;14mfrom[0m August 2008 [38;5;14mto[0m August 2009 ( `` [38;5;10msolar[0m [38;5;10mminimum[0m '' [38;5;10mperiod[0m with [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mvague[0m 27-day [38;5;6msolar[0m [38;5;6mcycle[0m ) . We demonstrate , for the first [38;5;14mtime[0m , that in the [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m the [38;5;10mdaily[0m [38;5;13mtime[0m [38;5;13mseries[0m of [38;5;1mOH[0m [38;5;10mconcentrations[0m [38;5;9mcorrelate[0m [38;5;13mwell[0m with the [38;5;1msolar[0m [38;5;1mirradiance[0m ( [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m [38;5;13mcoefficients[0m [38;5;13mup[0m [38;5;14mto[0m 0.79 ) at zero time-lag . At the same [38;5;14mtime[0m [38;5;8mH2O[0m anticorrelates ( [38;5;9mcorrelation[0m [38;5;13mcoefficients[0m [38;5;13mup[0m [38;5;14mto[0m −0.74 ) with the [38;5;1msolar[0m [38;5;1mirradiance[0m at non-zero time-lag . We found that the response of [38;5;1mOH[0m and [38;5;8mH2O[0m [38;5;14mto[0m the 27-day [38;5;6mvariability[0m of the [38;5;1msolar[0m [38;5;1mirradiance[0m is [38;5;10mstrong[0m for the [38;5;10mperiod[0m of the [38;5;10mhigh[0m [38;5;6msolar[0m [38;5;6mactivity[0m and negligible for the [38;5;10msolar[0m [38;5;10mminimum[0m [38;5;9mconditions[0m . It allows us [38;5;14mto[0m suggest that the 27-day [38;5;9mcycle[0m in the [38;5;1msolar[0m [38;5;1mirradiance[0m and in [38;5;1mOH[0m and [38;5;8mH2O[0m are [38;5;11mphysically[0m [38;5;9mconnected[0m .

Improved [38;5;13msimulation[0m of [38;5;1mtropospheric[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m by [38;5;7ma[0m global-multi-regional two-way [38;5;10mcoupling[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;6msystem[0m . Abstract . Small-scale [38;5;13mnonlinear[0m [38;5;8mchemical[0m and [38;5;12mphysical[0m [38;5;12mprocesses[0m over [38;5;6mpollution[0m [38;5;13msource[0m [38;5;10mregions[0m affect the [38;5;1mtropospheric[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m ( [38;5;1mO3[0m ) , but these [38;5;11mprocesses[0m are not captured by [38;5;12mcurrent[0m [38;5;5mglobal[0m [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;1mtransport[0m [38;5;13mmodels[0m ( CTMs ) and chemistry–climate [38;5;13mmodels[0m that are limited by [38;5;10mcoarse[0m [38;5;13mhorizontal[0m [38;5;13mresolutions[0m ( 100–500 km , [38;5;10mtypically[0m 200 km ) . These [38;5;13mmodels[0m tend [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;9mcontain[0m [38;5;10mlarge[0m ( and mostly [38;5;9mpositive[0m ) [38;5;5mtropospheric[0m [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;9mbiases[0m in the [38;5;5mNorthern[0m [38;5;5mHemisphere[0m . Here we [38;5;14muse[0m the [38;5;10mrecently[0m built two-way [38;5;10mcoupling[0m [38;5;6msystem[0m of the [38;5;4mGEOS-Chem[0m CTM [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;13msimulate[0m the [38;5;10mregional[0m and [38;5;5mglobal[0m [38;5;5mtropospheric[0m [38;5;1mO3[0m in 2009 . The [38;5;6msystem[0m [38;5;10mcouples[0m the [38;5;5mglobal[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m ( at 2.5° [38;5;10mlong[0m . × 2° lat . ) and its three nested [38;5;13mmodels[0m ( at 0.667° [38;5;10mlong[0m . × 0.5° lat . ) [38;5;7mcovering[0m [38;5;5mAsia[0m , [38;5;5mNorth[0m [38;5;5mAmerica[0m and [38;5;5mEurope[0m , respectively . Specifically , the nested [38;5;13mmodels[0m take [38;5;9mlateral[0m [38;5;10mboundary[0m [38;5;9mconditions[0m ( LBCs ) [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;5mglobal[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m , better capture small-scale [38;5;11mprocesses[0m and [38;5;6mfeed[0m back [38;5;14mto[0m modify the [38;5;5mglobal[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;13msimulation[0m within the nested domains , with [38;5;7ma[0m subsequent effect on their LBCs . Compared [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;5mglobal[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m alone , the two-way [38;5;10mcoupled[0m [38;5;6msystem[0m better [38;5;13msimulates[0m the [38;5;5mtropospheric[0m [38;5;1mO3[0m both within and [38;5;14moutside[0m the nested domains , [38;5;8mas[0m found by [38;5;11mevaluation[0m against [38;5;7ma[0m suite of [38;5;7mground[0m ( 1420 sites [38;5;14mfrom[0m the World [38;5;13mData[0m Centre for Greenhouse [38;5;1mGases[0m ( WDCGG ) , the [38;5;5mUnited[0m [38;5;5mStates[0m National [38;5;10mOceanic[0m and [38;5;10mAtmospheric[0m Administration ( NOAA ) [38;5;7mEarth[0m [38;5;6mSystem[0m [38;5;10mResearch[0m Laboratory [38;5;5mGlobal[0m [38;5;11mMonitoring[0m [38;5;13mDivision[0m ( GMD ) , the [38;5;8mChemical[0m [38;5;13mCoordination[0m Centre of European [38;5;11mMonitoring[0m and [38;5;11mEvaluation[0m Programme ( EMEP ) , and the [38;5;5mUnited[0m [38;5;5mStates[0m [38;5;11mEnvironmental[0m [38;5;11mProtection[0m [38;5;11mAgency[0m [38;5;6mAir[0m [38;5;6mQuality[0m [38;5;6mSystem[0m ( AQS ) ) , [38;5;8maircraft[0m ( the High-performance [38;5;8mInstrumented[0m [38;5;10mAirborne[0m [38;5;8mPlatform[0m for Environmental [38;5;10mResearch[0m ( HIAPER ) Pole-to-Pole [38;5;11mObservations[0m ( HIPPO ) and [38;5;13mMeasurement[0m of [38;5;1mOzone[0m and [38;5;1mWater[0m [38;5;1mVapor[0m by Airbus In- [38;5;11mService[0m [38;5;8mAircraft[0m ( MOZAIC ) ) and [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m ( two [38;5;1mOzone[0m [38;5;2mMonitoring[0m [38;5;2mInstrument[0m ( [38;5;2mOMI[0m ) [38;5;9mproducts[0m ) . Abstract . [38;5;10mPast[0m studies have shown that [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mclear[0m relationship exists between the [38;5;13mfield[0m of [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;13mpassive[0m tracer and the [38;5;13mProbability[0m [38;5;13mDistribution[0m [38;5;13mFunction[0m ( [38;5;13mPDF[0m ) of tracer [38;5;10mconcentrations[0m , which can [38;5;8mbe[0m exploited [38;5;14mto[0m identify the [38;5;9mposition[0m and [38;5;6mvariability[0m of [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;10mbarriers[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;10misentropic[0m [38;5;6mmixing[0m . In the [38;5;10mpresent[0m study , we [38;5;9mfocus[0m on the [38;5;11mdynamical[0m [38;5;10mbarrier[0m [38;5;9mlocated[0m in the [38;5;7msubtropics[0m . We calculate PDFs of the long-lived tracers [38;5;1mnitrous[0m [38;5;1moxide[0m ( [38;5;1mN2O[0m ) and [38;5;1mmethane[0m ( [38;5;1mCH4[0m ) [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;11mdifferent[0m [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;8minstruments[0m : the [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) on board [38;5;4mAura[0m , the [38;5;2mMichelson[0m [38;5;2mInterferometer[0m [38;5;2mfor[0m [38;5;2mPassive[0m [38;5;2mAtmospheric[0m [38;5;1mSounding[0m ( [38;5;2mMIPAS[0m ) on board Envisat , the Sub-Millimetre Radiometre ( [38;5;2mSMR[0m ) on board Odin and the [38;5;2mHalogen[0m [38;5;2mOccultation[0m [38;5;2mExperiment[0m ( [38;5;2mHALOE[0m ) on board [38;5;4mUARS[0m , overall [38;5;7mcovering[0m the [38;5;9mtime[0m [38;5;9mperiod[0m of 1992–2009 . An [38;5;11manalysis[0m of the [38;5;9mconsistency[0m among the [38;5;11mdifferent[0m [38;5;13msets[0m of [38;5;13mdata[0m and their capability of identifying [38;5;6mmixing[0m [38;5;10mregions[0m and barrier-to-transport [38;5;10mregions[0m in the [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m and the [38;5;7msubtropical[0m [38;5;10mbarrier[0m [38;5;9mlocation[0m is [38;5;7ma[0m prime aim of the [38;5;10mpresent[0m study . This is done looking at the [38;5;9mmorphological[0m [38;5;13mstructure[0m of the one- and two-dimensional PDFs of tracer [38;5;10mconcentrations[0m [38;5;14mmeasured[0m [38;5;14mby[0m the [38;5;11mdifferent[0m [38;5;8minstruments[0m . The latter [38;5;11mdiffer[0m in their spatial and temporal [38;5;13msampling[0m and [38;5;13mresolution[0m , and there are some systematic [38;5;11mdifferences[0m in the determination of the [38;5;7msubtropical[0m [38;5;10mbarrier[0m [38;5;9mposition[0m that have been highlighted . However , the four [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;8minstruments[0m offer an overall [38;5;9mconsistent[0m picture of the [38;5;7msubtropical[0m [38;5;10mbarrier[0m [38;5;6mannual[0m [38;5;6mcycle[0m . There is [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mstrong[0m [38;5;10mseasonality[0m [38;5;9mconsistently[0m [38;5;10mrepresented[0m , characterized by the wintertime [38;5;6mshift[0m of the [38;5;7msubtropical[0m [38;5;10medge[0m toward the [38;5;13msummer[0m [38;5;13mhemisphere[0m . However , the influence of the [38;5;6mQuasi[0m [38;5;6mBiennial[0m [38;5;1mOscillation[0m ( [38;5;1mQBO[0m ) on [38;5;10misentropic[0m [38;5;1mtransport[0m and [38;5;6mmixing[0m , and by consequence , on the [38;5;9mposition[0m of the [38;5;7msubtropical[0m [38;5;10mbarrier[0m , is not [38;5;14mequally[0m [38;5;10mrepresented[0m in all [38;5;7msatellite[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;14musing[0m the [38;5;13mmethodology[0m proposed .

This [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;13mset[0m is [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;5mglobal[0m long-term [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;7mEarth[0m [38;5;6msystem[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;13mrecord[0m , [38;5;9mconsisting[0m of [38;5;10mmonthly[0m [38;5;10mzonal[0m [38;5;9mmean[0m [38;5;13mtime[0m [38;5;13mseries[0m [38;5;14mstarting[0m [38;5;8mas[0m early [38;5;8mas[0m 1979 . Since the late 1990s , [38;5;1mHCl[0m [38;5;14mdecreases[0m [38;5;14min[0m the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m have occurred with pronounced latitudinal [38;5;6mvariability[0m at [38;5;9mrates[0m sometimes exceeding 1–2 % yr−1 . [38;5;10mRecent[0m short-term [38;5;9mtendencies[0m of lower-stratospheric and [38;5;13mcolumn[0m [38;5;1mHCl[0m vary substantially , with [38;5;14mincreases[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m 2005 [38;5;14mto[0m 2010 for northern midlatitudes and [38;5;10mdeep[0m [38;5;5mtropics[0m , but [38;5;14mdecreases[0m ( [38;5;14mincreases[0m ) after 2011 at northern ( southern ) midlatitudes . < [38;5;8mbr[0m > < [38;5;8mbr[0m > For [38;5;8mH2O[0m , the GOZCARDS [38;5;9mproduct[0m [38;5;7mcovers[0m both [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m and [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m , and the same [38;5;8minstruments[0m [38;5;8mas[0m for [38;5;1mHCl[0m are [38;5;14mused[0m , along with [38;5;4mUpper[0m [38;5;4mAtmosphere[0m [38;5;4mResearch[0m [38;5;4mSatellite[0m ( [38;5;4mUARS[0m ) [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;8mH2O[0m [38;5;13mdata[0m ( 1991–1993 ) . In the [38;5;10mupper[0m [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m , the anticorrelation between [38;5;8mH2O[0m and [38;5;1msolar[0m [38;5;1mflux[0m is now [38;5;10mclearly[0m [38;5;1mvisible[0m over two [38;5;10mfull[0m [38;5;6msolar[0m [38;5;6mcycles[0m . Are EEP [38;5;6mEvents[0m [38;5;10mImportant[0m for the [38;5;10mTertiary[0m [38;5;1mOzone[0m [38;5;9mMaximum[0m ? . [38;5;8mEnergetic[0m [38;5;8mparticle[0m [38;5;6mprecipitation[0m ( EPP ) [38;5;14mincreases[0m the [38;5;9mproduction[0m of odd [38;5;8mhydrogen[0m ( [38;5;8mHOX[0m ) [38;5;8mspecies[0m in the [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m , which catalytically destroy [38;5;1mozone[0m ( [38;5;1mO3[0m ) in [38;5;6msunlight[0m . Hence , the EPP‐HOX [38;5;14mimpact[0m on the [38;5;10mtertiary[0m [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;9mmaximum[0m ( TOM ) [38;5;10mdepends[0m on [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mcomplex[0m geometry of [38;5;7ma[0m geographic‐oriented TOM , geomagnetic‐oriented auroral [38;5;13mzone[0m , [38;5;10mproducing[0m short‐lived [38;5;8mHOX[0m [38;5;8mspecies[0m , and [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mdestruction[0m [38;5;11mprocess[0m [38;5;10mdepending[0m on the solar [38;5;9mzenith[0m [38;5;9mangle[0m ( SZA ) . [38;5;10mParticle[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;10mMedium[0m [38;5;9mEnergy[0m [38;5;8mProton[0m and [38;5;10mElectron[0m Detectors [38;5;8mtelescopes[0m aboard the [38;5;4mPolar[0m [38;5;4mOrbiting[0m [38;5;4mEnvironmental[0m [38;5;4mSatellites[0m , and [38;5;1mhydroxyl[0m ( [38;5;1mOH[0m ) and [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;9mmixing[0m [38;5;9mratios[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;10mmicrowave[0m limb sounder ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) are [38;5;14mused[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;11minvestigate[0m the [38;5;9mpotential[0m limitations of [38;5;14musing[0m the [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m [38;5;14mto[0m study EPP‐OH [38;5;14mimpact[0m on the TOM in the [38;5;5mNorthern[0m [38;5;5mHemisphere[0m . Our [38;5;11mresults[0m show limited [38;5;14moverlap[0m between the auroral [38;5;13mzone[0m and the TOM at [38;5;13mtwilight[0m [38;5;9mconditions[0m . [38;5;7mA[0m [38;5;1mcomposite[0m [38;5;11manalysis[0m [38;5;10mindicates[0m [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;9mmixing[0m [38;5;9mratio[0m [38;5;14mdecrease[0m over the auroral [38;5;13mzone[0m [38;5;6mlagged[0m by ∼1 [38;5;13mday[0m compared [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;9mmaximum[0m energetic [38;5;10melectron[0m [38;5;6mprecipitation[0m ( EEP ) ‐OH [38;5;14mimpact[0m . Hence , [38;5;2mMLS[0m is predominantly [38;5;11mobserving[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;6mlagged[0m and [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;14mestimate[0m [38;5;14mof[0m the response of [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;14mto[0m EEP‐OH at SZA > 95° . The EEP [38;5;14mimpact[0m [38;5;10mregion[0m within the TOM is smaller than the [38;5;14moverlap[0m [38;5;10mregion[0m , [38;5;10mstrongly[0m modulated by the [38;5;13mbackground[0m [38;5;10matmospheric[0m [38;5;11mdynamics[0m . The [38;5;11mresults[0m , although limited by the [38;5;7msatellites[0m viewing [38;5;9mconditions[0m , imply that the [38;5;10mimportance[0m of EEP upon [38;5;1mO3[0m [38;5;9mmixing[0m [38;5;9mratio[0m is [38;5;10mstrongly[0m influenced by the [38;5;13mbackground[0m [38;5;10matmosphere[0m , both in terms of [38;5;11mchemistry[0m and [38;5;11mdynamics[0m . Multisatellite [38;5;11mobservations[0m at [38;5;11mdifferent[0m solar [38;5;13mlocal[0m [38;5;13mtimes[0m are required [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;10mseparate[0m the [38;5;13mdirect[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;6mlagged[0m EEP‐OH [38;5;14mimpact[0m on [38;5;8mO3[0m .

Technical note : [38;5;13mReanalysis[0m of [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m . Abstract . This paper [38;5;10mpresents[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;13mreanalysis[0m of the [38;5;10matmospheric[0m [38;5;1mchemical[0m [38;5;1mcomposition[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;10mupper[0m [38;5;5mtroposphere[0m [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m August 2004 [38;5;14mto[0m December 2017 . This [38;5;13mreanalysis[0m is [38;5;10mproduced[0m by the Belgian [38;5;13mAssimilation[0m [38;5;6mSystem[0m for [38;5;8mChemical[0m [38;5;11mObsErvations[0m ( BASCOE ) constrained by the [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) on board the [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;7msatellite[0m . BASCOE is [38;5;14mbased[0m [38;5;14mon[0m the [38;5;13mensemble[0m Kalman [38;5;10mfilter[0m ( EnKF ) method and includes [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;1mtransport[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m driven by the [38;5;6mwinds[0m and [38;5;9mtemperature[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the ERA-Interim [38;5;11mmeteorological[0m [38;5;13mreanalysis[0m . The [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;13mresolution[0m is 3.75∘ in [38;5;13mlongitude[0m , 2.5∘ in [38;5;13mlatitude[0m and 37 [38;5;13mvertical[0m [38;5;9mlevels[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;13msurface[0m [38;5;14mto[0m 0.1 hPa with 25 [38;5;9mlevels[0m [38;5;14mabove[0m 100 hPa . The [38;5;13moutputs[0m are [38;5;10mprovided[0m every 6 h. This [38;5;13mreanalysis[0m is called BRAM2 for BASCOE [38;5;13mReanalysis[0m of [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m , [38;5;13mversion[0m 2 . [38;5;1mVertical[0m [38;5;1mprofiles[0m of eight [38;5;8mspecies[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;13mversion[0m 4 are [38;5;13massimilated[0m and are [38;5;11mevaluated[0m in this paper : [38;5;1mozone[0m ( [38;5;1mO3[0m ) , [38;5;8mwater[0m vapour ( [38;5;8mH2O[0m ) , [38;5;1mnitrous[0m [38;5;1moxide[0m ( [38;5;1mN2O[0m ) , [38;5;1mnitric[0m [38;5;1macid[0m ( [38;5;1mHNO3[0m ) , [38;5;1mhydrogen[0m [38;5;1mchloride[0m ( [38;5;1mHCl[0m ) , [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;1moxide[0m ( [38;5;1mClO[0m ) , [38;5;1mmethyl[0m [38;5;1mchloride[0m ( [38;5;1mCH3Cl[0m ) and [38;5;1mcarbon[0m [38;5;1mmonoxide[0m ( [38;5;1mCO[0m ) . They are [38;5;11mevaluated[0m [38;5;14musing[0m [38;5;10mindependent[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;2mAtmospheric[0m [38;5;2mChemistry[0m [38;5;2mExperiment[0m [38;5;2mFourier[0m [38;5;2mTransform[0m [38;5;2mSpectrometer[0m ( [38;5;2mACE-FTS[0m ) , the [38;5;2mMichelson[0m [38;5;2mInterferometer[0m [38;5;2mfor[0m [38;5;2mPassive[0m [38;5;2mAtmospheric[0m [38;5;1mSounding[0m ( [38;5;2mMIPAS[0m ) , the Superconducting Submillimeter-Wave Limb-Emission Sounder ( SMILES ) and [38;5;1mN2O[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;11mdifferent[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m radiometer than the one [38;5;14mused[0m [38;5;14mto[0m deliver the [38;5;11mstandard[0m [38;5;9mproduct[0m and ozonesondes . The [38;5;11mevaluation[0m is carried out in four [38;5;10mregions[0m of interest where only [38;5;6mselected[0m [38;5;8mspecies[0m are [38;5;11mevaluated[0m . These [38;5;10mregions[0m are ( 1 ) the lower-stratospheric [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m where [38;5;1mO3[0m , [38;5;8mH2O[0m , [38;5;1mN2O[0m , [38;5;1mHNO3[0m , [38;5;1mHCl[0m and [38;5;1mClO[0m are [38;5;11mevaluated[0m ; ( 2 ) the upper-stratospheric–lower-mesospheric [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m where [38;5;8mH2O[0m , [38;5;1mN2O[0m , [38;5;1mHNO3[0m and [38;5;1mCO[0m are [38;5;11mevaluated[0m ; ( 3 ) the [38;5;10mupper[0m troposphere–lower [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m ( UTLS ) where [38;5;1mO3[0m , [38;5;8mH2O[0m , [38;5;1mCO[0m and [38;5;1mCH3Cl[0m are [38;5;11mevaluated[0m ; and ( 4 ) the [38;5;10mmiddle[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m where [38;5;1mO3[0m , [38;5;8mH2O[0m , [38;5;1mN2O[0m , [38;5;1mHNO3[0m , [38;5;1mHCl[0m , [38;5;1mClO[0m and [38;5;1mCH3Cl[0m are [38;5;11mevaluated[0m . In [38;5;13mgeneral[0m BRAM2 reproduces [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m within their [38;5;10muncertainties[0m and agrees [38;5;13mwell[0m with [38;5;10mindependent[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m , with [38;5;10mseveral[0m limitations discussed in this paper ( see the summary in Sect . 5.5 ) . In particular , [38;5;1mozone[0m is not [38;5;13massimilated[0m at [38;5;9maltitudes[0m [38;5;14mabove[0m ( i.e . [38;5;10mpressures[0m [38;5;10mlower[0m than ) 4 hPa [38;5;14mdue[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;13mmodel[0m [38;5;9mbias[0m that can not [38;5;8mbe[0m [38;5;11mcorrected[0m by the [38;5;13massimilation[0m . [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;13mprofiles[0m display unphysical [38;5;1moscillations[0m in the [38;5;5mtropical[0m UTLS , which are [38;5;11mcorrected[0m by the [38;5;13massimilation[0m , allowing [38;5;7ma[0m good agreement with ozonesondes . Moreover , in the [38;5;10mupper[0m [38;5;5mtroposphere[0m , comparison of BRAM2 with [38;5;2mMLS[0m and [38;5;10mindependent[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m suggests [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;9mpositive[0m [38;5;9mbias[0m in [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;1mO3[0m and [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mnegative[0m [38;5;9mbias[0m in [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;8mH2O[0m . The [38;5;13mreanalysis[0m also reveals [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;6mdrift[0m in [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;1mN2O[0m against [38;5;10mindependent[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m , which highlights the [38;5;9mpotential[0m [38;5;14muse[0m of BRAM2 [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;13mestimate[0m [38;5;9mbiases[0m between [38;5;8minstruments[0m . BRAM2 is [38;5;11mpublicly[0m available and will [38;5;8mbe[0m extended [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;13massimilate[0m [38;5;2mMLS[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m after 2017 .

The [38;5;10mmajor[0m [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m final [38;5;10mwarming[0m in 2016 : [38;5;1mdispersal[0m of [38;5;6mvortex[0m [38;5;8mair[0m and [38;5;10mtermination[0m of [38;5;5mArctic[0m [38;5;8mchemical[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;6mloss[0m . Abstract . The 2015/16 [38;5;5mNorthern[0m [38;5;5mHemisphere[0m [38;5;13mwinter[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m appeared [38;5;14mto[0m have the greatest [38;5;9mpotential[0m yet seen for [38;5;13mrecord[0m [38;5;5mArctic[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;6mloss[0m . [38;5;9mTemperatures[0m in the [38;5;5mArctic[0m [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m were at [38;5;13mrecord[0m [38;5;10mlows[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m December 2015 through early February 2016 , with an unprecedented [38;5;10mperiod[0m of [38;5;9mtemperatures[0m [38;5;14mbelow[0m [38;5;6mice[0m [38;5;1mpolar[0m [38;5;1mstratospheric[0m [38;5;1mcloud[0m [38;5;9mthresholds[0m . [38;5;8mTrace[0m [38;5;8mgas[0m [38;5;13mmeasurements[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) show that exceptional [38;5;6mdenitrification[0m and [38;5;12mdehydration[0m , [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;13mwell[0m [38;5;8mas[0m [38;5;6mextensive[0m [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;6mactivation[0m , occurred throughout the [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m . [38;5;1mOzone[0m [38;5;14mdecreases[0m [38;5;14min[0m 2015/16 began earlier and proceeded more [38;5;10mrapidly[0m than those in 2010/11 , [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;13mwinter[0m that saw unprecedented [38;5;5mArctic[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;6mloss[0m . However , on 5–6 March 2016 [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mmajor[0m final sudden [38;5;5mstratospheric[0m [38;5;10mwarming[0m ( `` [38;5;10mmajor[0m final [38;5;10mwarming[0m '' , MFW ) began . By mid-March , the mid-stratospheric [38;5;6mvortex[0m split after [38;5;8mbeing[0m [38;5;6mdisplaced[0m [38;5;10mfar[0m off the [38;5;7mpole[0m . The [38;5;11mresulting[0m offspring [38;5;1mvortices[0m [38;5;6mdecayed[0m [38;5;10mrapidly[0m preceding the [38;5;10mfull[0m breakdown of the [38;5;6mvortex[0m by early April . In the [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m , the [38;5;10mperiod[0m of [38;5;9mtemperatures[0m [38;5;10mlow[0m enough for [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;6mactivation[0m [38;5;14mended[0m [38;5;10mnearly[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mmonth[0m earlier than that in 2011 because of the MFW . [38;5;1mOzone[0m [38;5;6mloss[0m [38;5;9mrates[0m were thus kept in check because there was less [38;5;6msunlight[0m during the [38;5;10mcold[0m [38;5;10mperiod[0m . SPE-induced [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;6mactivation[0m has been identified . [38;5;1mHCl[0m [38;5;14mdecrease[0m occurred at [38;5;10mnearly[0m all the [38;5;11minvestigated[0m [38;5;9maltitudes[0m ( i.e. , 10–0.5 hPa ) with the strongest [38;5;14mdecrease[0m ( of about 0.25 [38;5;13mppbv[0m ) on 21 January . [38;5;8mHOCl[0m was found [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mbe[0m the [38;5;5mmain[0m [38;5;6mactive[0m [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;8mspecies[0m [38;5;14munder[0m [38;5;13mnighttime[0m [38;5;9mconditions[0m ( with [38;5;14mincreases[0m of more than 0.2 [38;5;13mppbv[0m ) whereas both [38;5;8mHOCl[0m and [38;5;1mClO[0m enhancements ( about 0.1 [38;5;13mppbv[0m ) have been [38;5;11mobserved[0m at the [38;5;5mpolar[0m night [38;5;10mterminator[0m . Further , [38;5;10msmall[0m [38;5;1mClO[0m [38;5;14mdecreases[0m ( of [38;5;14mless[0m [38;5;14mthan[0m 0.1 [38;5;13mppbv[0m ) and [38;5;8mClONO2[0m enhancements ( about 0.2 [38;5;13mppbv[0m ) have been [38;5;11mobserved[0m at higher [38;5;13mlatitudes[0m ( i.e. , at [38;5;13mnighttime[0m ) [38;5;9mroughly[0m [38;5;14mabove[0m 2 hPa . While WACCM4 reproduces most of the SPE-induced [38;5;6mvariability[0m in the [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;8mspecies[0m fairly [38;5;13mwell[0m , in some particular [38;5;10mregions[0m [38;5;10mdiscrepancies[0m between the [38;5;13mmodeled[0m and [38;5;13mmeasured[0m temporal [38;5;6mevolution[0m of the [38;5;9mabundances[0m of [38;5;8mchlorine[0m [38;5;8mspecies[0m were found . [38;5;8mHOCl[0m [38;5;6mchanges[0m are [38;5;13mmodelled[0m [38;5;10mvery[0m [38;5;13mwell[0m [38;5;14mwith[0m [38;5;14mrespect[0m [38;5;14mto[0m both magnitude and [38;5;13mgeographic[0m distribution . [38;5;1mClO[0m [38;5;14mdecreases[0m are reproduced at [38;5;7mhigh[0m [38;5;7mlatitudes[0m , whereas [38;5;1mClO[0m enhancements in the [38;5;10mterminator[0m [38;5;10mregion[0m are underestimated and [38;5;11mattributed[0m [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;13mbackground[0m [38;5;6mvariations[0m . WACCM4 also reproduces the [38;5;1mHCl[0m depletion in the [38;5;5mmesosphere[0m but it does not show the [38;5;11mobserved[0m [38;5;14mdecrease[0m [38;5;14mbelow[0m about 2 hPa . The [38;5;6muptake[0m of [38;5;1mHO2[0m on [38;5;8mmeteoric[0m [38;5;1msmoke[0m analogues . The kinetics of [38;5;10mheterogeneous[0m [38;5;1mHO2[0m [38;5;6muptake[0m onto [38;5;8mmeteoric[0m [38;5;1msmoke[0m [38;5;10mparticles[0m ( MSPs ) has been studied in the laboratory [38;5;14musing[0m analogues of [38;5;2mMSP[0m [38;5;8maerosol[0m [38;5;1mentrained[0m into [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;6mflow[0m [38;5;13mtube[0m . The [38;5;6muptake[0m [38;5;13mcoefficient[0m , γ , was determined on synthetic [38;5;10mamorphous[0m olivine ( MgFeSiO4 ) [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mbe[0m ( 6.9 ± 1.2 ) × 10−2 at [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;1mrelative[0m [38;5;1mhumidity[0m ( RH ) of 10 % . On forsterite ( Mg2SiO4 ) , γ = ( 4.3 ± 0.4 ) × 10−3 at RH = 11.6 % and ( 7.3 ± 0.4 ) × 10−2 at RH = 9.9 % on fayalite ( Fe2SiO4 ) . These [38;5;11mresults[0m [38;5;10mindicate[0m that [38;5;8mFe[0m plays [38;5;7ma[0m more [38;5;10mimportant[0m mechanistic [38;5;9mrole[0m than [38;5;8mMg[0m in the [38;5;6mremoval[0m of [38;5;1mHO2[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the [38;5;10mgas[0m phase . [38;5;10mElectronic[0m [38;5;13mstructure[0m calculations show that [38;5;8mFe[0m [38;5;8matoms[0m exposed at the [38;5;10mparticle[0m [38;5;13msurface[0m [38;5;10mprovide[0m [38;5;7ma[0m catalytic site where [38;5;1mHO2[0m is converted [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;8mH2O2[0m via an Eley-Rideal [38;5;11mmechanism[0m , but this does not occur on exposed [38;5;13msurface[0m [38;5;8mMg[0m [38;5;8matoms[0m . The [38;5;14mimpact[0m of this [38;5;10mheterogeneous[0m [38;5;11mprocess[0m in the [38;5;7mmiddle[0m [38;5;7matmosphere[0m was then [38;5;11minvestigated[0m [38;5;14musing[0m [38;5;7ma[0m whole [38;5;10matmosphere[0m chemistry-climate [38;5;13mmodel[0m which incorporates [38;5;7ma[0m microphysical [38;5;11mtreatment[0m of MSPs . [38;5;14mUsing[0m [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;5mglobal[0m [38;5;2mMSP[0m [38;5;9mproduction[0m [38;5;9mrate[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;8mmeteoric[0m [38;5;1mablation[0m of 44 t/day , [38;5;10mheterogeneous[0m [38;5;6muptake[0m ( with γ = 0.2 ) on MSPs [38;5;10msignificantly[0m alters the [38;5;8mHOx[0m [38;5;9mbudget[0m in the [38;5;13mnighttime[0m [38;5;5mpolar[0m [38;5;6mvortex[0m . [38;5;11mEvaluation[0m of the [38;5;13mACCESS[0m – chemistry–climate [38;5;13mmodel[0m for the [38;5;5mSouthern[0m [38;5;5mHemisphere[0m . Abstract . [38;5;1mvertical[0m [38;5;1mprofiles[0m of [38;5;1mozone[0m and [38;5;9mtemperature[0m with ozonesonde [38;5;13mdata[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m [38;5;5mAustralia[0m , [38;5;5mNew[0m [38;5;5mZealand[0m and [38;5;5mAntarctica[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m 38 [38;5;14mto[0m 90° S. [38;5;10mExcess[0m [38;5;1mozone[0m [38;5;10mconcentrations[0m ( [38;5;14mgreater[0m The [38;5;13mmodel[0m 's inability [38;5;14mto[0m [38;5;13mexplicitly[0m [38;5;13msimulate[0m [38;5;7ma[0m supercooled ternary [38;5;13msolution[0m may also explain the lack of depletion at [38;5;10mlower[0m [38;5;9maltitudes[0m . [38;5;11mAnalysis[0m of the [38;5;13msimulated[0m Southern Annular [38;5;9mMode[0m ( SAM ) [38;5;9mindex[0m compares [38;5;13mwell[0m with ERA-Interim [38;5;13mdata[0m , an [38;5;10mimportant[0m [38;5;9mmetric[0m for [38;5;11mcorrect[0m [38;5;14mrepresentation[0m [38;5;14mof[0m Australian [38;5;6mclimate[0m . [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m of biomass-burning [38;5;9mproducts[0m [38;5;14mfrom[0m the Australian bush [38;5;6mfires[0m of February 2009 . Abstract . The [38;5;10mlarge[0m bush [38;5;6mfires[0m which occurred in southeast [38;5;5mAustralia[0m in February 2009 were [38;5;10munusually[0m [38;5;10mdestructive[0m . However , they were also [38;5;10munusual[0m in the amounts of various [38;5;12mcombustion[0m [38;5;9mproducts[0m which were injected [38;5;13mdirectly[0m into the [38;5;5mstratosphere[0m . We report the [38;5;11mobservations[0m by the [38;5;2mMicrowave[0m [38;5;2mLimb[0m [38;5;2mSounder[0m ( [38;5;2mMLS[0m ) [38;5;8minstrument[0m on the [38;5;4mAura[0m [38;5;7msatellite[0m of some of these [38;5;12mcombustion[0m [38;5;9mproducts[0m . The highest [38;5;9mquality[0m [38;5;11mobservations[0m are of [38;5;1mCO[0m ; these [38;5;10mclearly[0m show [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mlarge[0m [38;5;10mregion[0m of enhanced [38;5;9mmixing[0m [38;5;9mratios[0m [38;5;14mto[0m the [38;5;13mnorth[0m of [38;5;5mNew[0m [38;5;5mZealand[0m which remains in that [38;5;10mregion[0m for about ten [38;5;13mdays[0m before [38;5;6mdrifting[0m [38;5;13mwestwards[0m and finally [38;5;12mdissipating[0m over the Atlantic about [38;5;7ma[0m [38;5;10mmonth[0m after the [38;5;6mfire[0m .
